02926  */
02927 static struct slist *
02928 gen_off_macpl(void)
02929 {
02930     struct slist *s;
02931 
02932     if (off_macpl_is_variable) {
02933         if (reg_off_macpl == -1) {
02934             /*
02935              * We haven't yet assigned a register for the offset
02936              * of the MAC-layer payload; allocate one.
02937              */
02938             reg_off_macpl = alloc_reg();
02939         }
02940 
02941         /*
02942          * Load the register containing the offset of the MAC-layer
02943          * payload into the X register.
02944          */
02945         s = new_stmt(BPF_LDX|BPF_MEM);
02946         s->s.k = reg_off_macpl;
02947         return s;
02948     } else {
02949         /*
02950          * That offset isn't variable, so we don't need to
02951          * generate any code.
02952          */
02953         return NULL;
02954     }
02955 }
02956 
02957 /*
02958  * Map an Ethernet type to the equivalent PPP type.
02959  */
02960 static int
02961 ethertype_to_ppptype(proto)
02962     int proto;
02963 {
02964     switch (proto) {
02965 
02966     case ETHERTYPE_IP:
02967         proto = PPP_IP;
02968         break;
02969 
02970 #ifdef INET6
02971     case ETHERTYPE_IPV6:
02972         proto = PPP_IPV6;
02973         break;
02974 #endif
02975 
02976     case ETHERTYPE_DN:
02977         proto = PPP_DECNET;
02978         break;
02979 
02980     case ETHERTYPE_ATALK:
02981         proto = PPP_APPLE;
02982         break;
02983 
02984     case ETHERTYPE_NS:
02985         proto = PPP_NS;
02986         break;
02987 
02988     case LLCSAP_ISONS:
02989         proto = PPP_OSI;
02990         break;
02991 
02992     case LLCSAP_8021D:
02993         /*
02994          * I'm assuming the "Bridging PDU"s that go
02995          * over PPP are Spanning Tree Protocol
02996          * Bridging PDUs.
02997          */
02998         proto = PPP_BRPDU;
02999         break;
03000 
03001     case LLCSAP_IPX:
03002         proto = PPP_IPX;
03003         break;
03004     }
03005     return (proto);
03006 }
03007 
03008 /*
03009  * Generate code to match a particular packet type by matching the
03010  * link-layer type field or fields in the 802.2 LLC header.
03011  *
03012  * "proto" is an Ethernet type value, if > ETHERMTU, or an LLC SAP
03013  * value, if <= ETHERMTU.
03014  */
03015 static struct block *
03016 gen_linktype(proto)
03017     register int proto;
03018 {
03019     struct block *b0, *b1, *b2;
03020 
03021     /* are we checking MPLS-encapsulated packets? */
03022     if (label_stack_depth > 0) {
03023         switch (proto) {
03024         case ETHERTYPE_IP:
03025         case PPP_IP:
03026             /* FIXME add other L3 proto IDs */
03027             return gen_mpls_linktype(Q_IP); 
03028 
03029         case ETHERTYPE_IPV6:
03030         case PPP_IPV6:
03031             /* FIXME add other L3 proto IDs */
03032             return gen_mpls_linktype(Q_IPV6); 
03033 
03034         default:
03035             bpf_error("unsupported protocol over mpls");
03036             /* NOTREACHED */
03037         }
03038     }
03039 
03040     /*
03041      * Are we testing PPPoE packets?
03042      */
03043     if (is_pppoes) {
03044         /*
03045          * The PPPoE session header is part of the
03046          * MAC-layer payload, so all references
03047          * should be relative to the beginning of
03048          * that payload.
03049          */
03050 
03051         /*
03052          * We use Ethernet protocol types inside libpcap;
03053          * map them to the corresponding PPP protocol types.
03054          */
03055         proto = ethertype_to_ppptype(proto);
03056         return gen_cmp(OR_MACPL, off_linktype, BPF_H, (bpf_int32)proto);
03057     }
03058 
03059     switch (linktype) {
03060 
03061     case DLT_EN10MB:
03062         return gen_ether_linktype(proto);
03063         /*NOTREACHED*/
03064         break;
03065 
03066     case DLT_C_HDLC:
03067         switch (proto) {
03068 
03069         case LLCSAP_ISONS:
03070             proto = (proto << 8 | LLCSAP_ISONS);
03071             /* fall through */
03072 
03073         default:
03074             return gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_H,
03075                 (bpf_int32)proto);
03076             /*NOTREACHED*/
03077             break;
03078         }
03079         break;
03080 
03081     case DLT_IEEE802_11:
03082     case DLT_PRISM_HEADER:
03083     case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO_AVS:
03084     case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO:
03085     case DLT_PPI:
03086         /*
03087          * Check that we have a data frame.
03088          */
03089         b0 = gen_check_802_11_data_frame();
03090 
03091         /*
03092          * Now check for the specified link-layer type.
03093          */
03094         b1 = gen_llc_linktype(proto);
03095         gen_and(b0, b1);
03096         return b1;
03097         /*NOTREACHED*/
03098         break;
03099 
03100     case DLT_FDDI:
03101         /*
03102          * XXX - check for asynchronous frames, as per RFC 1103.
03103          */
03104         return gen_llc_linktype(proto);
03105         /*NOTREACHED*/
03106         break;
03107 
03108     case DLT_IEEE802:
03109         /*
03110          * XXX - check for LLC PDUs, as per IEEE 802.5.
03111          */
03112         return gen_llc_linktype(proto);
03113         /*NOTREACHED*/
03114         break;
03115 
03116     case DLT_ATM_RFC1483:
03117     case DLT_ATM_CLIP:
03118     case DLT_IP_OVER_FC:
03119         return gen_llc_linktype(proto);
03120         /*NOTREACHED*/
03121         break;
03122 
03123     case DLT_SUNATM:
03124         /*
03125          * If "is_lane" is set, check for a LANE-encapsulated
03126          * version of this protocol, otherwise check for an
03127          * LLC-encapsulated version of this protocol.
03128          *
03129          * We assume LANE means Ethernet, not Token Ring.
03130          */
03131         if (is_lane) {
03132             /*
03133              * Check that the packet doesn't begin with an
03134              * LE Control marker.  (We've already generated
03135              * a test for LANE.)
03136              */
03137             b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, SUNATM_PKT_BEGIN_POS, BPF_H,
03138                 0xFF00);
03139             gen_not(b0);
03140 
03141             /*
03142              * Now generate an Ethernet test.
03143              */
03144             b1 = gen_ether_linktype(proto);
03145             gen_and(b0, b1);
03146             return b1;
03147         } else {
03148             /*
03149              * Check for LLC encapsulation and then check the
03150              * protocol.
03151              */
03152             b0 = gen_atmfield_code(A_PROTOTYPE, PT_LLC, BPF_JEQ, 0);
03153             b1 = gen_llc_linktype(proto);
03154             gen_and(b0, b1);
03155             return b1;
03156         }
03157         /*NOTREACHED*/
03158         break;
03159 
03160     case DLT_LINUX_SLL:
03161         return gen_linux_sll_linktype(proto);
03162         /*NOTREACHED*/
03163         break;
03164 
03165     case DLT_SLIP:
03166     case DLT_SLIP_BSDOS:
03167     case DLT_RAW:
03168         /*
03169          * These types don't provide any type field; packets
03170          * are always IPv4 or IPv6.
03171          *
03172          * XXX - for IPv4, check for a version number of 4, and,
03173          * for IPv6, check for a version number of 6?
03174          */
03175         switch (proto) {
03176 
03177         case ETHERTYPE_IP:
03178             /* Check for a version number of 4. */
03179             return gen_mcmp(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B, 0x40, 0xF0);
03180 #ifdef INET6
03181         case ETHERTYPE_IPV6:
03182             /* Check for a version number of 6. */
03183             return gen_mcmp(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B, 0x60, 0xF0);
03184 #endif
03185 
03186         default:
03187             return gen_false();     /* always false */
03188         }
03189         /*NOTREACHED*/
03190         break;
03191 
03192     case DLT_IPV4:
03193         /*
03194          * Raw IPv4, so no type field.
03195          */
03196         if (proto == ETHERTYPE_IP)
03197             return gen_true();      /* always true */
03198 
03199         /* Checking for something other than IPv4; always false */
03200         return gen_false();
03201         /*NOTREACHED*/
03202         break;
03203 
03204     case DLT_IPV6:
03205         /*
03206          * Raw IPv6, so no type field.
03207          */
03208 #ifdef INET6
03209         if (proto == ETHERTYPE_IPV6)
03210             return gen_true();      /* always true */
03211 #endif
03212 
03213         /* Checking for something other than IPv6; always false */
03214         return gen_false();
03215         /*NOTREACHED*/
03216         break;
03217 
03218     case DLT_PPP:
03219     case DLT_PPP_PPPD:
03220     case DLT_PPP_SERIAL:
03221     case DLT_PPP_ETHER:
03222         /*
03223          * We use Ethernet protocol types inside libpcap;
03224          * map them to the corresponding PPP protocol types.
03225          */
03226         proto = ethertype_to_ppptype(proto);
03227         return gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_H, (bpf_int32)proto);
03228         /*NOTREACHED*/
03229         break;
03230 
03231     case DLT_PPP_BSDOS:
03232         /*
03233          * We use Ethernet protocol types inside libpcap;
03234          * map them to the corresponding PPP protocol types.
03235          */
03236         switch (proto) {
03237 
03238         case ETHERTYPE_IP:
03239             /*
03240              * Also check for Van Jacobson-compressed IP.
03241              * XXX - do this for other forms of PPP?
03242              */
03243             b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_H, PPP_IP);
03244             b1 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_H, PPP_VJC);
03245             gen_or(b0, b1);
03246             b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_H, PPP_VJNC);
03247             gen_or(b1, b0);
03248             return b0;
03249 
03250         default:
03251             proto = ethertype_to_ppptype(proto);
03252             return gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_H,
03253                 (bpf_int32)proto);
03254         }
03255         /*NOTREACHED*/
03256         break;
03257 
03258     case DLT_NULL:
03259     case DLT_LOOP:
03260     case DLT_ENC:
03261         /*
03262          * For DLT_NULL, the link-layer header is a 32-bit
03263          * word containing an AF_ value in *host* byte order,
03264          * and for DLT_ENC, the link-layer header begins
03265          * with a 32-bit work containing an AF_ value in
03266          * host byte order.
03267          *
03268          * In addition, if we're reading a saved capture file,
03269          * the host byte order in the capture may not be the
03270          * same as the host byte order on this machine.
03271          *
03272          * For DLT_LOOP, the link-layer header is a 32-bit
03273          * word containing an AF_ value in *network* byte order.
03274          *
03275          * XXX - AF_ values may, unfortunately, be platform-
03276          * dependent; for example, FreeBSD's AF_INET6 is 24
03277          * whilst NetBSD's and OpenBSD's is 26.
03278          *
03279          * This means that, when reading a capture file, just
03280          * checking for our AF_INET6 value won't work if the
03281          * capture file came from another OS.
03282          */
03283         switch (proto) {
03284 
03285         case ETHERTYPE_IP:
03286             proto = AF_INET;
03287             break;
03288 
03289 #ifdef INET6
03290         case ETHERTYPE_IPV6:
03291             proto = AF_INET6;
03292             break;
03293 #endif
03294 
03295         default:
03296             /*
03297              * Not a type on which we support filtering.
03298              * XXX - support those that have AF_ values
03299              * #defined on this platform, at least?
03300              */
03301             return gen_false();
03302         }
03303 
03304         if (linktype == DLT_NULL || linktype == DLT_ENC) {
03305             /*
03306              * The AF_ value is in host byte order, but
03307              * the BPF interpreter will convert it to
03308              * network byte order.
03309              *
03310              * If this is a save file, and it's from a
03311              * machine with the opposite byte order to
03312              * ours, we byte-swap the AF_ value.
03313              *
03314              * Then we run it through "htonl()", and
03315              * generate code to compare against the result.
03316              */
03317             if (bpf_pcap->sf.rfile != NULL &&
03318                 bpf_pcap->sf.swapped)
03319                 proto = SWAPLONG(proto);
03320             proto = htonl(proto);
03321         }
03322         return (gen_cmp(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_W, (bpf_int32)proto));
03323 
03324 #ifdef HAVE_NET_PFVAR_H
03325     case DLT_PFLOG:
03326         /*
03327          * af field is host byte order in contrast to the rest of
03328          * the packet.
03329          */
03330         if (proto == ETHERTYPE_IP)
03331             return (gen_cmp(OR_LINK, offsetof(struct pfloghdr, af),
03332                 BPF_B, (bpf_int32)AF_INET));
03333 #ifdef INET6
03334         else if (proto == ETHERTYPE_IPV6)
03335             return (gen_cmp(OR_LINK, offsetof(struct pfloghdr, af),
03336                 BPF_B, (bpf_int32)AF_INET6));
03337 #endif /* INET6 */
03338         else
03339             return gen_false();
03340         /*NOTREACHED*/
03341         break;
03342 #endif /* HAVE_NET_PFVAR_H */
03343 
03344     case DLT_ARCNET:
03345     case DLT_ARCNET_LINUX:
03346         /*
03347          * XXX should we check for first fragment if the protocol
03348          * uses PHDS?
03349          */
03350         switch (proto) {
03351 
03352         default:
03353             return gen_false();
03354 
03355 #ifdef INET6
03356         case ETHERTYPE_IPV6:
03357             return (gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_B,
03358                 (bpf_int32)ARCTYPE_INET6));
03359 #endif /* INET6 */
03360 
03361         case ETHERTYPE_IP:
03362             b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_B,
03363                      (bpf_int32)ARCTYPE_IP);
03364             b1 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_B,
03365                      (bpf_int32)ARCTYPE_IP_OLD);
03366             gen_or(b0, b1);
03367             return (b1);
03368 
03369         case ETHERTYPE_ARP:
03370             b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_B,
03371                      (bpf_int32)ARCTYPE_ARP);
03372             b1 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_B,
03373                      (bpf_int32)ARCTYPE_ARP_OLD);
03374             gen_or(b0, b1);
03375             return (b1);
03376 
03377         case ETHERTYPE_REVARP:
03378             return (gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_B,
03379                     (bpf_int32)ARCTYPE_REVARP));
03380 
03381         case ETHERTYPE_ATALK:
03382             return (gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_B,
03383                     (bpf_int32)ARCTYPE_ATALK));
03384         }
03385         /*NOTREACHED*/
03386         break;
03387 
03388     case DLT_LTALK:
03389         switch (proto) {
03390         case ETHERTYPE_ATALK:
03391             return gen_true();
03392         default:
03393             return gen_false();
03394         }
03395         /*NOTREACHED*/
03396         break;
03397 
03398     case DLT_FRELAY:
03399         /*
03400          * XXX - assumes a 2-byte Frame Relay header with
03401          * DLCI and flags.  What if the address is longer?
03402          */
03403         switch (proto) {
03404 
03405         case ETHERTYPE_IP:
03406             /*
03407              * Check for the special NLPID for IP.
03408              */
03409             return gen_cmp(OR_LINK, 2, BPF_H, (0x03<<8) | 0xcc);
03410 
03411 #ifdef INET6
03412         case ETHERTYPE_IPV6:
03413             /*
03414              * Check for the special NLPID for IPv6.
03415              */
03416             return gen_cmp(OR_LINK, 2, BPF_H, (0x03<<8) | 0x8e);
03417 #endif
03418 
03419         case LLCSAP_ISONS:
03420             /*
03421              * Check for several OSI protocols.
03422              *
03423              * Frame Relay packets typically have an OSI
03424              * NLPID at the beginning; we check for each
03425              * of them.
03426              *
03427              * What we check for is the NLPID and a frame
03428              * control field of UI, i.e. 0x03 followed
03429              * by the NLPID.
03430              */
03431             b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, 2, BPF_H, (0x03<<8) | ISO8473_CLNP);
03432             b1 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, 2, BPF_H, (0x03<<8) | ISO9542_ESIS);
03433             b2 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, 2, BPF_H, (0x03<<8) | ISO10589_ISIS);
03434             gen_or(b1, b2);
03435             gen_or(b0, b2);
03436             return b2;
03437 
03438         default:
03439             return gen_false();
03440         }
03441         /*NOTREACHED*/
03442         break;
03443 
03444     case DLT_MFR:
03445         bpf_error("Multi-link Frame Relay link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03446 
03447         case DLT_JUNIPER_MFR:
03448         case DLT_JUNIPER_MLFR:
03449         case DLT_JUNIPER_MLPPP:
03450     case DLT_JUNIPER_ATM1:
03451     case DLT_JUNIPER_ATM2:
03452     case DLT_JUNIPER_PPPOE:
03453     case DLT_JUNIPER_PPPOE_ATM:
03454         case DLT_JUNIPER_GGSN:
03455         case DLT_JUNIPER_ES:
03456         case DLT_JUNIPER_MONITOR:
03457         case DLT_JUNIPER_SERVICES:
03458         case DLT_JUNIPER_ETHER:
03459         case DLT_JUNIPER_PPP:
03460         case DLT_JUNIPER_FRELAY:
03461         case DLT_JUNIPER_CHDLC:
03462         case DLT_JUNIPER_VP:
03463         case DLT_JUNIPER_ST:
03464         case DLT_JUNIPER_ISM:
03465         /* just lets verify the magic number for now -
03466          * on ATM we may have up to 6 different encapsulations on the wire
03467          * and need a lot of heuristics to figure out that the payload
03468          * might be;
03469          *
03470          * FIXME encapsulation specific BPF_ filters
03471          */
03472         return gen_mcmp(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_W, 0x4d474300, 0xffffff00); /* compare the magic number */
03473 
03474     case DLT_IPNET:
03475         return gen_ipnet_linktype(proto);
03476 
03477     case DLT_LINUX_IRDA:
03478         bpf_error("IrDA link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03479 
03480     case DLT_DOCSIS:
03481         bpf_error("DOCSIS link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03482 
03483     case DLT_MTP2:
03484     case DLT_MTP2_WITH_PHDR:
03485         bpf_error("MTP2 link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03486 
03487     case DLT_ERF:
03488         bpf_error("ERF link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03489 
03490 #ifdef DLT_PFSYNC
03491     case DLT_PFSYNC:
03492         bpf_error("PFSYNC link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03493 #endif
03494 
03495     case DLT_LINUX_LAPD:
03496         bpf_error("LAPD link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03497 
03498     case DLT_USB:
03499     case DLT_USB_LINUX:
03500     case DLT_USB_LINUX_MMAPPED:
03501         bpf_error("USB link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03502 
03503     case DLT_BLUETOOTH_HCI_H4:
03504     case DLT_BLUETOOTH_HCI_H4_WITH_PHDR:
03505         bpf_error("Bluetooth link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03506 
03507     case DLT_CAN20B:
03508     case DLT_CAN_SOCKETCAN:
03509         bpf_error("CAN link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03510 
03511     case DLT_IEEE802_15_4:
03512     case DLT_IEEE802_15_4_LINUX:
03513     case DLT_IEEE802_15_4_NONASK_PHY:
03514         bpf_error("IEEE 802.15.4 link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03515 
03516     case DLT_IEEE802_16_MAC_CPS_RADIO:
03517         bpf_error("IEEE 802.16 link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03518 
03519     case DLT_SITA:
03520         bpf_error("SITA link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03521 
03522     case DLT_RAIF1:
03523         bpf_error("RAIF1 link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03524 
03525     case DLT_IPMB:
03526         bpf_error("IPMB link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03527 
03528     case DLT_AX25_KISS:
03529         bpf_error("AX.25 link-layer type filtering not implemented");
03530     }
03531 
03532     /*
03533      * All the types that have no encapsulation should either be
03534      * handled as DLT_SLIP, DLT_SLIP_BSDOS, and DLT_RAW are, if
03535      * all packets are IP packets, or should be handled in some
03536      * special case, if none of them are (if some are and some
03537      * aren't, the lack of encapsulation is a problem, as we'd
03538      * have to find some other way of determining the packet type).
03539      *
03540      * Therefore, if "off_linktype" is -1, there's an error.
03541      */
03542     if (off_linktype == (u_int)-1)
03543         abort();
03544 
03545     /*
03546      * Any type not handled above should always have an Ethernet
03547      * type at an offset of "off_linktype".
03548      */
03549     return gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_H, (bpf_int32)proto);
03550 }
03551 
03552 /*
03553  * Check for an LLC SNAP packet with a given organization code and
03554  * protocol type; we check the entire contents of the 802.2 LLC and
03555  * snap headers, checking for DSAP and SSAP of SNAP and a control
03556  * field of 0x03 in the LLC header, and for the specified organization
03557  * code and protocol type in the SNAP header.
03558  */
03559 static struct block *
03560 gen_snap(orgcode, ptype)
03561     bpf_u_int32 orgcode;
03562     bpf_u_int32 ptype;
03563 {
03564     u_char snapblock[8];
03565 
03566     snapblock[0] = LLCSAP_SNAP; /* DSAP = SNAP */
03567     snapblock[1] = LLCSAP_SNAP; /* SSAP = SNAP */
03568     snapblock[2] = 0x03;        /* control = UI */
03569     snapblock[3] = (orgcode >> 16); /* upper 8 bits of organization code */
03570     snapblock[4] = (orgcode >> 8);  /* middle 8 bits of organization code */
03571     snapblock[5] = (orgcode >> 0);  /* lower 8 bits of organization code */
03572     snapblock[6] = (ptype >> 8);    /* upper 8 bits of protocol type */
03573     snapblock[7] = (ptype >> 0);    /* lower 8 bits of protocol type */
03574     return gen_bcmp(OR_MACPL, 0, 8, snapblock);
03575 }
03576 
03577 /*
03578  * Generate code to match a particular packet type, for link-layer types
03579  * using 802.2 LLC headers.
03580  *
03581  * This is *NOT* used for Ethernet; "gen_ether_linktype()" is used
03582  * for that - it handles the D/I/X Ethernet vs. 802.3+802.2 issues.
03583  *
03584  * "proto" is an Ethernet type value, if > ETHERMTU, or an LLC SAP
03585  * value, if <= ETHERMTU.  We use that to determine whether to
03586  * match the DSAP or both DSAP and LSAP or to check the OUI and
03587  * protocol ID in a SNAP header.
03588  */
03589 static struct block *
03590 gen_llc_linktype(proto)
03591     int proto;
03592 {
03593     /*
03594      * XXX - handle token-ring variable-length header.
03595      */
03596     switch (proto) {
03597 
03598     case LLCSAP_IP:
03599     case LLCSAP_ISONS:
03600     case LLCSAP_NETBEUI:
03601         /*
03602          * XXX - should we check both the DSAP and the
03603          * SSAP, like this, or should we check just the
03604          * DSAP, as we do for other types <= ETHERMTU
03605          * (i.e., other SAP values)?
03606          */
03607         return gen_cmp(OR_MACPL, 0, BPF_H, (bpf_u_int32)
03608                  ((proto << 8) | proto));
03609 
03610     case LLCSAP_IPX:
03611         /*
03612          * XXX - are there ever SNAP frames for IPX on
03613          * non-Ethernet 802.x networks?
03614          */
03615         return gen_cmp(OR_MACPL, 0, BPF_B,
03616             (bpf_int32)LLCSAP_IPX);
03617 
03618     case ETHERTYPE_ATALK:
03619         /*
03620          * 802.2-encapsulated ETHERTYPE_ATALK packets are
03621          * SNAP packets with an organization code of
03622          * 0x080007 (Apple, for Appletalk) and a protocol
03623          * type of ETHERTYPE_ATALK (Appletalk).
03624          *
03625          * XXX - check for an organization code of
03626          * encapsulated Ethernet as well?
03627          */
03628         return gen_snap(0x080007, ETHERTYPE_ATALK);
03629 
03630     default:
03631         /*
03632          * XXX - we don't have to check for IPX 802.3
03633          * here, but should we check for the IPX Ethertype?
03634          */
03635         if (proto <= ETHERMTU) {
03636             /*
03637              * This is an LLC SAP value, so check
03638              * the DSAP.
03639              */
03640             return gen_cmp(OR_MACPL, 0, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)proto);
03641         } else {
03642             /*
03643              * This is an Ethernet type; we assume that it's
03644              * unlikely that it'll appear in the right place
03645              * at random, and therefore check only the
03646              * location that would hold the Ethernet type
03647              * in a SNAP frame with an organization code of
03648              * 0x000000 (encapsulated Ethernet).
03649              *
03650              * XXX - if we were to check for the SNAP DSAP and
03651              * LSAP, as per XXX, and were also to check for an
03652              * organization code of 0x000000 (encapsulated
03653              * Ethernet), we'd do
03654              *
03655              *  return gen_snap(0x000000, proto);
03656              *
03657              * here; for now, we don't, as per the above.
03658              * I don't know whether it's worth the extra CPU
03659              * time to do the right check or not.
03660              */
03661             return gen_cmp(OR_MACPL, 6, BPF_H, (bpf_int32)proto);
03662         }
03663     }
03664 }
03665 
03666 static struct block *
03667 gen_hostop(addr, mask, dir, proto, src_off, dst_off)
03668     bpf_u_int32 addr;
03669     bpf_u_int32 mask;
03670     int dir, proto;
03671     u_int src_off, dst_off;
03672 {
03673     struct block *b0, *b1;
03674     u_int offset;
03675 
03676     switch (dir) {
03677 
03678     case Q_SRC:
03679         offset = src_off;
03680         break;
03681 
03682     case Q_DST:
03683         offset = dst_off;
03684         break;
03685 
03686     case Q_AND:
03687         b0 = gen_hostop(addr, mask, Q_SRC, proto, src_off, dst_off);
03688         b1 = gen_hostop(addr, mask, Q_DST, proto, src_off, dst_off);
03689         gen_and(b0, b1);
03690         return b1;
03691 
03692     case Q_OR:
03693     case Q_DEFAULT:
03694         b0 = gen_hostop(addr, mask, Q_SRC, proto, src_off, dst_off);
03695         b1 = gen_hostop(addr, mask, Q_DST, proto, src_off, dst_off);
03696         gen_or(b0, b1);
03697         return b1;
03698 
03699     default:
03700         abort();
03701     }
03702     b0 = gen_linktype(proto);
03703     b1 = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, offset, BPF_W, (bpf_int32)addr, mask);
03704     gen_and(b0, b1);
03705     return b1;
03706 }
03707 
03708 #ifdef INET6
03709 static struct block *
03710 gen_hostop6(addr, mask, dir, proto, src_off, dst_off)
03711     struct in6_addr *addr;
03712     struct in6_addr *mask;
03713     int dir, proto;
03714     u_int src_off, dst_off;
03715 {
03716     struct block *b0, *b1;
03717     u_int offset;
03718     u_int32_t *a, *m;
03719 
03720     switch (dir) {
03721 
03722     case Q_SRC:
03723         offset = src_off;
03724         break;
03725 
03726     case Q_DST:
03727         offset = dst_off;
03728         break;
03729 
03730     case Q_AND:
03731         b0 = gen_hostop6(addr, mask, Q_SRC, proto, src_off, dst_off);
03732         b1 = gen_hostop6(addr, mask, Q_DST, proto, src_off, dst_off);
03733         gen_and(b0, b1);
03734         return b1;
03735 
03736     case Q_OR:
03737     case Q_DEFAULT:
03738         b0 = gen_hostop6(addr, mask, Q_SRC, proto, src_off, dst_off);
03739         b1 = gen_hostop6(addr, mask, Q_DST, proto, src_off, dst_off);
03740         gen_or(b0, b1);
03741         return b1;
03742 
03743     default:
03744         abort();
03745     }
03746     /* this order is important */
03747     a = (u_int32_t *)addr;
03748     m = (u_int32_t *)mask;
03749     b1 = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, offset + 12, BPF_W, ntohl(a[3]), ntohl(m[3]));
03750     b0 = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, offset + 8, BPF_W, ntohl(a[2]), ntohl(m[2]));
03751     gen_and(b0, b1);
03752     b0 = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, offset + 4, BPF_W, ntohl(a[1]), ntohl(m[1]));
03753     gen_and(b0, b1);
03754     b0 = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, offset + 0, BPF_W, ntohl(a[0]), ntohl(m[0]));
03755     gen_and(b0, b1);
03756     b0 = gen_linktype(proto);
03757     gen_and(b0, b1);
03758     return b1;
03759 }
03760 #endif /*INET6*/
03761 
03762 static struct block *
03763 gen_ehostop(eaddr, dir)
03764     register const u_char *eaddr;
03765     register int dir;
03766 {
03767     register struct block *b0, *b1;
03768 
03769     switch (dir) {
03770     case Q_SRC:
03771         return gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, off_mac + 6, 6, eaddr);
03772 
03773     case Q_DST:
03774         return gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, off_mac + 0, 6, eaddr);
03775 
03776     case Q_AND:
03777         b0 = gen_ehostop(eaddr, Q_SRC);
03778         b1 = gen_ehostop(eaddr, Q_DST);
03779         gen_and(b0, b1);
03780         return b1;
03781 
03782     case Q_DEFAULT:
03783     case Q_OR:
03784         b0 = gen_ehostop(eaddr, Q_SRC);
03785         b1 = gen_ehostop(eaddr, Q_DST);
03786         gen_or(b0, b1);
03787         return b1;
03788     }
03789     abort();
03790     /* NOTREACHED */
03791 }
03792 
03793 /*
03794  * Like gen_ehostop, but for DLT_FDDI
03795  */
03796 static struct block *
03797 gen_fhostop(eaddr, dir)
03798     register const u_char *eaddr;
03799     register int dir;
03800 {
03801     struct block *b0, *b1;
03802 
03803     switch (dir) {
03804     case Q_SRC:
03805 #ifdef PCAP_FDDIPAD
03806         return gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 6 + 1 + pcap_fddipad, 6, eaddr);
03807 #else
03808         return gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 6 + 1, 6, eaddr);
03809 #endif
03810 
03811     case Q_DST:
03812 #ifdef PCAP_FDDIPAD
03813         return gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 0 + 1 + pcap_fddipad, 6, eaddr);
03814 #else
03815         return gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 0 + 1, 6, eaddr);
03816 #endif
03817 
03818     case Q_AND:
03819         b0 = gen_fhostop(eaddr, Q_SRC);
03820         b1 = gen_fhostop(eaddr, Q_DST);
03821         gen_and(b0, b1);
03822         return b1;
03823 
03824     case Q_DEFAULT:
03825     case Q_OR:
03826         b0 = gen_fhostop(eaddr, Q_SRC);
03827         b1 = gen_fhostop(eaddr, Q_DST);
03828         gen_or(b0, b1);
03829         return b1;
03830     }
03831     abort();
03832     /* NOTREACHED */
03833 }
03834 
03835 /*
03836  * Like gen_ehostop, but for DLT_IEEE802 (Token Ring)
03837  */
03838 static struct block *
03839 gen_thostop(eaddr, dir)
03840     register const u_char *eaddr;
03841     register int dir;
03842 {
03843     register struct block *b0, *b1;
03844 
03845     switch (dir) {
03846     case Q_SRC:
03847         return gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 8, 6, eaddr);
03848 
03849     case Q_DST:
03850         return gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 2, 6, eaddr);
03851 
03852     case Q_AND:
03853         b0 = gen_thostop(eaddr, Q_SRC);
03854         b1 = gen_thostop(eaddr, Q_DST);
03855         gen_and(b0, b1);
03856         return b1;
03857 
03858     case Q_DEFAULT:
03859     case Q_OR:
03860         b0 = gen_thostop(eaddr, Q_SRC);
03861         b1 = gen_thostop(eaddr, Q_DST);
03862         gen_or(b0, b1);
03863         return b1;
03864     }
03865     abort();
03866     /* NOTREACHED */
03867 }
03868 
03869 /*
03870  * Like gen_ehostop, but for DLT_IEEE802_11 (802.11 wireless LAN) and
03871  * various 802.11 + radio headers.
03872  */
03873 static struct block *
03874 gen_wlanhostop(eaddr, dir)
03875     register const u_char *eaddr;
03876     register int dir;
03877 {
03878     register struct block *b0, *b1, *b2;
03879     register struct slist *s;
03880 
03881 #ifdef ENABLE_WLAN_FILTERING_PATCH
03882     /*
03883      * TODO GV 20070613
03884      * We need to disable the optimizer because the optimizer is buggy
03885      * and wipes out some LD instructions generated by the below
03886      * code to validate the Frame Control bits
03887      */
03888     no_optimize = 1;
03889 #endif /* ENABLE_WLAN_FILTERING_PATCH */
03890 
03891     switch (dir) {
03892     case Q_SRC:
03893         /*
03894          * Oh, yuk.
03895          *
03896          *  For control frames, there is no SA.
03897          *
03898          *  For management frames, SA is at an
03899          *  offset of 10 from the beginning of
03900          *  the packet.
03901          *
03902          *  For data frames, SA is at an offset
03903          *  of 10 from the beginning of the packet
03904          *  if From DS is clear, at an offset of
03905          *  16 from the beginning of the packet
03906          *  if From DS is set and To DS is clear,
03907          *  and an offset of 24 from the beginning
03908          *  of the packet if From DS is set and To DS
03909          *  is set.
03910          */
03911 
03912         /*
03913          * Generate the tests to be done for data frames
03914          * with From DS set.
03915          *
03916          * First, check for To DS set, i.e. check "link[1] & 0x01".
03917          */
03918         s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 1, BPF_B);
03919         b1 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
03920         b1->s.k = 0x01; /* To DS */
03921         b1->stmts = s;
03922 
03923         /*
03924          * If To DS is set, the SA is at 24.
03925          */
03926         b0 = gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 24, 6, eaddr);
03927         gen_and(b1, b0);
03928 
03929         /*
03930          * Now, check for To DS not set, i.e. check
03931          * "!(link[1] & 0x01)".
03932          */
03933         s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 1, BPF_B);
03934         b2 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
03935         b2->s.k = 0x01; /* To DS */
03936         b2->stmts = s;
03937         gen_not(b2);
03938 
03939         /*
03940          * If To DS is not set, the SA is at 16.
03941          */
03942         b1 = gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 16, 6, eaddr);
03943         gen_and(b2, b1);
03944 
03945         /*
03946          * Now OR together the last two checks.  That gives
03947          * the complete set of checks for data frames with
03948          * From DS set.
03949          */
03950         gen_or(b1, b0);
03951 
03952         /*
03953          * Now check for From DS being set, and AND that with
03954          * the ORed-together checks.
03955          */
03956         s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 1, BPF_B);
03957         b1 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
03958         b1->s.k = 0x02; /* From DS */
03959         b1->stmts = s;
03960         gen_and(b1, b0);
03961 
03962         /*
03963          * Now check for data frames with From DS not set.
03964          */
03965         s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 1, BPF_B);
03966         b2 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
03967         b2->s.k = 0x02; /* From DS */
03968         b2->stmts = s;
03969         gen_not(b2);
03970 
03971         /*
03972          * If From DS isn't set, the SA is at 10.
03973          */
03974         b1 = gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 10, 6, eaddr);
03975         gen_and(b2, b1);
03976 
03977         /*
03978          * Now OR together the checks for data frames with
03979          * From DS not set and for data frames with From DS
03980          * set; that gives the checks done for data frames.
03981          */
03982         gen_or(b1, b0);
03983 
03984         /*
03985          * Now check for a data frame.
03986          * I.e, check "link[0] & 0x08".
03987          */
03988         s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B);
03989         b1 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
03990         b1->s.k = 0x08;
03991         b1->stmts = s;
03992 
03993         /*
03994          * AND that with the checks done for data frames.
03995          */
03996         gen_and(b1, b0);
03997 
03998         /*
03999          * If the high-order bit of the type value is 0, this
04000          * is a management frame.
04001          * I.e, check "!(link[0] & 0x08)".
04002          */
04003         s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B);
04004         b2 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
04005         b2->s.k = 0x08;
04006         b2->stmts = s;
04007         gen_not(b2);
04008 
04009         /*
04010          * For management frames, the SA is at 10.
04011          */
04012         b1 = gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 10, 6, eaddr);
04013         gen_and(b2, b1);
04014 
04015         /*
04016          * OR that with the checks done for data frames.
04017          * That gives the checks done for management and
04018          * data frames.
04019          */
04020         gen_or(b1, b0);
04021 
04022         /*
04023          * If the low-order bit of the type value is 1,
04024          * this is either a control frame or a frame
04025          * with a reserved type, and thus not a
04026          * frame with an SA.
04027          *
04028          * I.e., check "!(link[0] & 0x04)".
04029          */
04030         s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B);
04031         b1 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
04032         b1->s.k = 0x04;
04033         b1->stmts = s;
04034         gen_not(b1);
04035 
04036         /*
04037          * AND that with the checks for data and management
04038          * frames.
04039          */
04040         gen_and(b1, b0);
04041         return b0;
04042 
04043     case Q_DST:
04044         /*
04045          * Oh, yuk.
04046          *
04047          *  For control frames, there is no DA.
04048          *
04049          *  For management frames, DA is at an
04050          *  offset of 4 from the beginning of
04051          *  the packet.
04052          *
04053          *  For data frames, DA is at an offset
04054          *  of 4 from the beginning of the packet
04055          *  if To DS is clear and at an offset of
04056          *  16 from the beginning of the packet
04057          *  if To DS is set.
04058          */
04059 
04060         /*
04061          * Generate the tests to be done for data frames.
04062          *
04063          * First, check for To DS set, i.e. "link[1] & 0x01".
04064          */
04065         s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 1, BPF_B);
04066         b1 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
04067         b1->s.k = 0x01; /* To DS */
04068         b1->stmts = s;
04069 
04070         /*
04071          * If To DS is set, the DA is at 16.
04072          */
04073         b0 = gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 16, 6, eaddr);
04074         gen_and(b1, b0);
04075 
04076         /*
04077          * Now, check for To DS not set, i.e. check
04078          * "!(link[1] & 0x01)".
04079          */
04080         s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 1, BPF_B);
04081         b2 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
04082         b2->s.k = 0x01; /* To DS */
04083         b2->stmts = s;
04084         gen_not(b2);
04085 
04086         /*
04087          * If To DS is not set, the DA is at 4.
04088          */
04089         b1 = gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 4, 6, eaddr);
04090         gen_and(b2, b1);
04091 
04092         /*
04093          * Now OR together the last two checks.  That gives
04094          * the complete set of checks for data frames.
04095          */
04096         gen_or(b1, b0);
04097 
04098         /*
04099          * Now check for a data frame.
04100          * I.e, check "link[0] & 0x08".
04101          */
04102         s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B);
04103         b1 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
04104         b1->s.k = 0x08;
04105         b1->stmts = s;
04106 
04107         /*
04108          * AND that with the checks done for data frames.
04109          */
04110         gen_and(b1, b0);
04111 
04112         /*
04113          * If the high-order bit of the type value is 0, this
04114          * is a management frame.
04115          * I.e, check "!(link[0] & 0x08)".
04116          */
04117         s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B);
04118         b2 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
04119         b2->s.k = 0x08;
04120         b2->stmts = s;
04121         gen_not(b2);
04122 
04123         /*
04124          * For management frames, the DA is at 4.
04125          */
04126         b1 = gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 4, 6, eaddr);
04127         gen_and(b2, b1);
04128 
04129         /*
04130          * OR that with the checks done for data frames.
04131          * That gives the checks done for management and
04132          * data frames.
04133          */
04134         gen_or(b1, b0);
04135 
04136         /*
04137          * If the low-order bit of the type value is 1,
04138          * this is either a control frame or a frame
04139          * with a reserved type, and thus not a
04140          * frame with an SA.
04141          *
04142          * I.e., check "!(link[0] & 0x04)".
04143          */
04144         s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B);
04145         b1 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
04146         b1->s.k = 0x04;
04147         b1->stmts = s;
04148         gen_not(b1);
04149 
04150         /*
04151          * AND that with the checks for data and management
04152          * frames.
04153          */
04154         gen_and(b1, b0);
04155         return b0;
04156 
04157     /*
04158      * XXX - add RA, TA, and BSSID keywords?
04159      */
04160     case Q_ADDR1:
04161         return (gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 4, 6, eaddr));
04162 
04163     case Q_ADDR2:
04164         /*
04165          * Not present in CTS or ACK control frames.
04166          */
04167         b0 = gen_mcmp(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B, IEEE80211_FC0_TYPE_CTL,
04168             IEEE80211_FC0_TYPE_MASK);
04169         gen_not(b0);
04170         b1 = gen_mcmp(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B, IEEE80211_FC0_SUBTYPE_CTS,
04171             IEEE80211_FC0_SUBTYPE_MASK);
04172         gen_not(b1);
04173         b2 = gen_mcmp(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B, IEEE80211_FC0_SUBTYPE_ACK,
04174             IEEE80211_FC0_SUBTYPE_MASK);
04175         gen_not(b2);
04176         gen_and(b1, b2);
04177         gen_or(b0, b2);
04178         b1 = gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 10, 6, eaddr);
04179         gen_and(b2, b1);
04180         return b1;
04181 
04182     case Q_ADDR3:
04183         /*
04184          * Not present in control frames.
04185          */
04186         b0 = gen_mcmp(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B, IEEE80211_FC0_TYPE_CTL,
04187             IEEE80211_FC0_TYPE_MASK);
04188         gen_not(b0);
04189         b1 = gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 16, 6, eaddr);
04190         gen_and(b0, b1);
04191         return b1;
04192 
04193     case Q_ADDR4:
04194         /*
04195          * Present only if the direction mask has both "From DS"
04196          * and "To DS" set.  Neither control frames nor management
04197          * frames should have both of those set, so we don't
04198          * check the frame type.
04199          */
04200         b0 = gen_mcmp(OR_LINK, 1, BPF_B,
04201             IEEE80211_FC1_DIR_DSTODS, IEEE80211_FC1_DIR_MASK);
04202         b1 = gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 24, 6, eaddr);
04203         gen_and(b0, b1);
04204         return b1;
04205 
04206     case Q_AND:
04207         b0 = gen_wlanhostop(eaddr, Q_SRC);
04208         b1 = gen_wlanhostop(eaddr, Q_DST);
04209         gen_and(b0, b1);
04210         return b1;
04211 
04212     case Q_DEFAULT:
04213     case Q_OR:
04214         b0 = gen_wlanhostop(eaddr, Q_SRC);
04215         b1 = gen_wlanhostop(eaddr, Q_DST);
04216         gen_or(b0, b1);
04217         return b1;
04218     }
04219     abort();
04220     /* NOTREACHED */
04221 }
04222 
04223 /*
04224  * Like gen_ehostop, but for RFC 2625 IP-over-Fibre-Channel.
04225  * (We assume that the addresses are IEEE 48-bit MAC addresses,
04226  * as the RFC states.)
04227  */
04228 static struct block *
04229 gen_ipfchostop(eaddr, dir)
04230     register const u_char *eaddr;
04231     register int dir;
04232 {
04233     register struct block *b0, *b1;
04234 
04235     switch (dir) {
04236     case Q_SRC:
04237         return gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 10, 6, eaddr);
04238 
04239     case Q_DST:
04240         return gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 2, 6, eaddr);
04241 
04242     case Q_AND:
04243         b0 = gen_ipfchostop(eaddr, Q_SRC);
04244         b1 = gen_ipfchostop(eaddr, Q_DST);
04245         gen_and(b0, b1);
04246         return b1;
04247 
04248     case Q_DEFAULT:
04249     case Q_OR:
04250         b0 = gen_ipfchostop(eaddr, Q_SRC);
04251         b1 = gen_ipfchostop(eaddr, Q_DST);
04252         gen_or(b0, b1);
04253         return b1;
04254     }
04255     abort();
04256     /* NOTREACHED */
04257 }
04258 
04259 /*
04260  * This is quite tricky because there may be pad bytes in front of the
04261  * DECNET header, and then there are two possible data packet formats that
04262  * carry both src and dst addresses, plus 5 packet types in a format that
04263  * carries only the src node, plus 2 types that use a different format and
04264  * also carry just the src node.
04265  *
04266  * Yuck.
04267  *
04268  * Instead of doing those all right, we just look for data packets with
04269  * 0 or 1 bytes of padding.  If you want to look at other packets, that
04270  * will require a lot more hacking.
04271  *
04272  * To add support for filtering on DECNET "areas" (network numbers)
04273  * one would want to add a "mask" argument to this routine.  That would
04274  * make the filter even more inefficient, although one could be clever
04275  * and not generate masking instructions if the mask is 0xFFFF.
04276  */
04277 static struct block *
04278 gen_dnhostop(addr, dir)
04279     bpf_u_int32 addr;
04280     int dir;
04281 {
04282     struct block *b0, *b1, *b2, *tmp;
04283     u_int offset_lh;    /* offset if long header is received */
04284     u_int offset_sh;    /* offset if short header is received */
04285 
04286     switch (dir) {
04287 
04288     case Q_DST:
04289         offset_sh = 1;  /* follows flags */
04290         offset_lh = 7;  /* flgs,darea,dsubarea,HIORD */
04291         break;
04292 
04293     case Q_SRC:
04294         offset_sh = 3;  /* follows flags, dstnode */
04295         offset_lh = 15; /* flgs,darea,dsubarea,did,sarea,ssub,HIORD */
04296         break;
04297 
04298     case Q_AND:
04299         /* Inefficient because we do our Calvinball dance twice */
04300         b0 = gen_dnhostop(addr, Q_SRC);
04301         b1 = gen_dnhostop(addr, Q_DST);
04302         gen_and(b0, b1);
04303         return b1;
04304 
04305     case Q_OR:
04306     case Q_DEFAULT:
04307         /* Inefficient because we do our Calvinball dance twice */
04308         b0 = gen_dnhostop(addr, Q_SRC);
04309         b1 = gen_dnhostop(addr, Q_DST);
04310         gen_or(b0, b1);
04311         return b1;
04312 
04313     case Q_ISO:
04314         bpf_error("ISO host filtering not implemented");
04315 
04316     default:
04317         abort();
04318     }
04319     b0 = gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_DN);
04320     /* Check for pad = 1, long header case */
04321     tmp = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, 2, BPF_H,
04322         (bpf_int32)ntohs(0x0681), (bpf_int32)ntohs(0x07FF));
04323     b1 = gen_cmp(OR_NET, 2 + 1 + offset_lh,
04324         BPF_H, (bpf_int32)ntohs((u_short)addr));
04325     gen_and(tmp, b1);
04326     /* Check for pad = 0, long header case */
04327     tmp = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, 2, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)0x06, (bpf_int32)0x7);
04328     b2 = gen_cmp(OR_NET, 2 + offset_lh, BPF_H, (bpf_int32)ntohs((u_short)addr));
04329     gen_and(tmp, b2);
04330     gen_or(b2, b1);
04331     /* Check for pad = 1, short header case */
04332     tmp = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, 2, BPF_H,
04333         (bpf_int32)ntohs(0x0281), (bpf_int32)ntohs(0x07FF));
04334     b2 = gen_cmp(OR_NET, 2 + 1 + offset_sh, BPF_H, (bpf_int32)ntohs((u_short)addr));
04335     gen_and(tmp, b2);
04336     gen_or(b2, b1);
04337     /* Check for pad = 0, short header case */
04338     tmp = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, 2, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)0x02, (bpf_int32)0x7);
04339     b2 = gen_cmp(OR_NET, 2 + offset_sh, BPF_H, (bpf_int32)ntohs((u_short)addr));
04340     gen_and(tmp, b2);
04341     gen_or(b2, b1);
04342 
04343     /* Combine with test for linktype */
04344     gen_and(b0, b1);
04345     return b1;
04346 }
04347 
04348 /*
04349  * Generate a check for IPv4 or IPv6 for MPLS-encapsulated packets;
04350  * test the bottom-of-stack bit, and then check the version number
04351  * field in the IP header.
04352  */
04353 static struct block *
04354 gen_mpls_linktype(proto)
04355     int proto;
04356 {
04357     struct block *b0, *b1;
04358 
04359         switch (proto) {
04360 
04361         case Q_IP:
04362                 /* match the bottom-of-stack bit */
04363                 b0 = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, -2, BPF_B, 0x01, 0x01);
04364                 /* match the IPv4 version number */
04365                 b1 = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, 0, BPF_B, 0x40, 0xf0);
04366                 gen_and(b0, b1);
04367                 return b1;
04368  
04369        case Q_IPV6:
04370                 /* match the bottom-of-stack bit */
04371                 b0 = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, -2, BPF_B, 0x01, 0x01);
04372                 /* match the IPv4 version number */
04373                 b1 = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, 0, BPF_B, 0x60, 0xf0);
04374                 gen_and(b0, b1);
04375                 return b1;
04376  
04377        default:
04378                 abort();
04379         }
04380 }
04381 
04382 static struct block *
04383 gen_host(addr, mask, proto, dir, type)
04384     bpf_u_int32 addr;
04385     bpf_u_int32 mask;
04386     int proto;
04387     int dir;
04388     int type;
04389 {
04390     struct block *b0, *b1;
04391     const char *typestr;
04392 
04393     if (type == Q_NET)
04394         typestr = "net";
04395     else
04396         typestr = "host";
04397 
04398     switch (proto) {
04399 
04400     case Q_DEFAULT:
04401         b0 = gen_host(addr, mask, Q_IP, dir, type);
04402         /*
04403          * Only check for non-IPv4 addresses if we're not
04404          * checking MPLS-encapsulated packets.
04405          */
04406         if (label_stack_depth == 0) {
04407             b1 = gen_host(addr, mask, Q_ARP, dir, type);
04408             gen_or(b0, b1);
04409             b0 = gen_host(addr, mask, Q_RARP, dir, type);
04410             gen_or(b1, b0);
04411         }
04412         return b0;
04413 
04414     case Q_IP:
04415         return gen_hostop(addr, mask, dir, ETHERTYPE_IP, 12, 16);
04416 
04417     case Q_RARP:
04418         return gen_hostop(addr, mask, dir, ETHERTYPE_REVARP, 14, 24);
04419 
04420     case Q_ARP:
04421         return gen_hostop(addr, mask, dir, ETHERTYPE_ARP, 14, 24);
04422 
04423     case Q_TCP:
04424         bpf_error("'tcp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04425 
04426     case Q_SCTP:
04427         bpf_error("'sctp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04428 
04429     case Q_UDP:
04430         bpf_error("'udp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04431 
04432     case Q_ICMP:
04433         bpf_error("'icmp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04434 
04435     case Q_IGMP:
04436         bpf_error("'igmp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04437 
04438     case Q_IGRP:
04439         bpf_error("'igrp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04440 
04441     case Q_PIM:
04442         bpf_error("'pim' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04443 
04444     case Q_VRRP:
04445         bpf_error("'vrrp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04446 
04447     case Q_ATALK:
04448         bpf_error("ATALK host filtering not implemented");
04449 
04450     case Q_AARP:
04451         bpf_error("AARP host filtering not implemented");
04452 
04453     case Q_DECNET:
04454         return gen_dnhostop(addr, dir);
04455 
04456     case Q_SCA:
04457         bpf_error("SCA host filtering not implemented");
04458 
04459     case Q_LAT:
04460         bpf_error("LAT host filtering not implemented");
04461 
04462     case Q_MOPDL:
04463         bpf_error("MOPDL host filtering not implemented");
04464 
04465     case Q_MOPRC:
04466         bpf_error("MOPRC host filtering not implemented");
04467 
04468 #ifdef INET6
04469     case Q_IPV6:
04470         bpf_error("'ip6' modifier applied to ip host");
04471 
04472     case Q_ICMPV6:
04473         bpf_error("'icmp6' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04474 #endif /* INET6 */
04475 
04476     case Q_AH:
04477         bpf_error("'ah' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04478 
04479     case Q_ESP:
04480         bpf_error("'esp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04481 
04482     case Q_ISO:
04483         bpf_error("ISO host filtering not implemented");
04484 
04485     case Q_ESIS:
04486         bpf_error("'esis' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04487 
04488     case Q_ISIS:
04489         bpf_error("'isis' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04490 
04491     case Q_CLNP:
04492         bpf_error("'clnp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04493 
04494     case Q_STP:
04495         bpf_error("'stp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04496 
04497     case Q_IPX:
04498         bpf_error("IPX host filtering not implemented");
04499 
04500     case Q_NETBEUI:
04501         bpf_error("'netbeui' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04502 
04503     case Q_RADIO:
04504         bpf_error("'radio' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04505 
04506     default:
04507         abort();
04508     }
04509     /* NOTREACHED */
04510 }
04511 
04512 #ifdef INET6
04513 static struct block *
04514 gen_host6(addr, mask, proto, dir, type)
04515     struct in6_addr *addr;
04516     struct in6_addr *mask;
04517     int proto;
04518     int dir;
04519     int type;
04520 {
04521     const char *typestr;
04522

04524         typestr = "net";
04525     else
04526         typestr = "host";

04532 
04533     case Q_IP:

04536     case Q_RARP:

04538 
04539     case Q_ARP:
04540         bpf_error("'arp' modifier applied to ip6 %s", typestr);
04541 
04542     case Q_SCTP:
04543         bpf_error("'sctp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04544 
04545     case Q_TCP:
04546         bpf_error("'tcp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04547 
04548     case Q_UDP:
04549         bpf_error("'udp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04550 
04551     case Q_ICMP:
04552         bpf_error("'icmp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04553 
04554     case Q_IGMP:
04555         bpf_error("'igmp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04556 
04557     case Q_IGRP:
04558         bpf_error("'igrp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04559 
04560     case Q_PIM:
04561         bpf_error("'pim' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04562 
04563     case Q_VRRP:
04564         bpf_error("'vrrp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04565 
04566     case Q_ATALK:
04567         bpf_error("ATALK host filtering not implemented");
04568 
04569     case Q_AARP:
04570         bpf_error("AARP host filtering not implemented");
04571 
04572     case Q_DECNET:
04573         bpf_error("'decnet' modifier applied to ip6 %s", typestr);
04574 
04575     case Q_SCA:

04577 
04578     case Q_LAT:
04579         bpf_error("LAT host filtering not implemented");
04580 
04581     case Q_MOPDL:
04582         bpf_error("MOPDL host filtering not implemented");
04583 
04584     case Q_MOPRC:
04585         bpf_error("MOPRC host filtering not implemented");

04589

04592 
04593     case Q_AH:

04595 
04596     case Q_ESP:

04598 
04599     case Q_ISO:
04600         bpf_error("ISO host filtering not implemented");
04601 
04602     case Q_ESIS:
04603         bpf_error("'esis' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04604 
04605     case Q_ISIS:
04606         bpf_error("'isis' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04607 
04608     case Q_CLNP:
04609         bpf_error("'clnp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04610 
04611     case Q_STP:
04612         bpf_error("'stp' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04613 
04614     case Q_IPX:
04615         bpf_error("IPX host filtering not implemented");
04616 
04617     case Q_NETBEUI:
04618         bpf_error("'netbeui' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04619 
04620     case Q_RADIO:
04621         bpf_error("'radio' modifier applied to %s", typestr);
04622

04625     }
04626     /* NOTREACHED */

04629 
04630 #ifndef INET6
04631 static struct block *
04632 gen_gateway(eaddr, alist, proto, dir)
04633     const u_char *eaddr;
04634     bpf_u_int32 **alist;
04635     int proto;
04636     int dir;
04637 {
04638     struct block *b0, *b1, *tmp;
04639 
04640     if (dir != 0)
04641         bpf_error("direction applied to 'gateway'");
04642 
04643     switch (proto) {
04644     case Q_DEFAULT:
04645     case Q_IP:
04646     case Q_ARP:
04647     case Q_RARP:
04648         switch (linktype) {
04649         case DLT_EN10MB:
04650             b0 = gen_ehostop(eaddr, Q_OR);
04651             break;
04652         case DLT_FDDI:
04653             b0 = gen_fhostop(eaddr, Q_OR);
04654             break;
04655         case DLT_IEEE802:
04656             b0 = gen_thostop(eaddr, Q_OR);
04657             break;
04658         case DLT_IEEE802_11:
04659         case DLT_PRISM_HEADER:
04660         case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO_AVS:
04661         case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO:
04662         case DLT_PPI:
04663             b0 = gen_wlanhostop(eaddr, Q_OR);
04664             break;
04665         case DLT_SUNATM:
04666             if (!is_lane)
04667                 bpf_error(
04668                     "'gateway' supported only on ethernet/FDDI/token ring/802.11/ATM LANE/Fibre Channel");
04669             /*
04670              * Check that the packet doesn't begin with an
04671              * LE Control marker.  (We've already generated
04672              * a test for LANE.)
04673              */
04674             b1 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, SUNATM_PKT_BEGIN_POS,
04675                 BPF_H, 0xFF00);
04676             gen_not(b1);
04677 
04678             /*
04679              * Now check the MAC address.
04680              */
04681             b0 = gen_ehostop(eaddr, Q_OR);
04682             gen_and(b1, b0);
04683             break;
04684         case DLT_IP_OVER_FC:
04685             b0 = gen_ipfchostop(eaddr, Q_OR);
04686             break;
04687         default:
04688             bpf_error(
04689                 "'gateway' supported only on ethernet/FDDI/token ring/802.11/ATM LANE/Fibre Channel");
04690         }
04691         b1 = gen_host(**alist++, 0xffffffff, proto, Q_OR, Q_HOST);
04692         while (*alist) {
04693             tmp = gen_host(**alist++, 0xffffffff, proto, Q_OR,
04694                 Q_HOST);
04695             gen_or(b1, tmp);
04696             b1 = tmp;
04697         }
04698         gen_not(b1);
04699         gen_and(b0, b1);
04700         return b1;
04701     }
04702     bpf_error("illegal modifier of 'gateway'");
04703     /* NOTREACHED */
04704 }
04705 #endif
04706 
04707 struct block *
04708 gen_proto_abbrev(proto)
04709     int proto;
04710 {
04711     struct block *b0;
04712     struct block *b1;
04713 
04714     switch (proto) {
04715 
04716     case Q_SCTP:
04717         b1 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_SCTP, Q_IP, Q_DEFAULT);
04718 #ifdef INET6
04719         b0 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_SCTP, Q_IPV6, Q_DEFAULT);
04720         gen_or(b0, b1);
04721 #endif
04722         break;
04723 
04724     case Q_TCP:
04725         b1 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_TCP, Q_IP, Q_DEFAULT);
04726 #ifdef INET6
04727         b0 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_TCP, Q_IPV6, Q_DEFAULT);
04728         gen_or(b0, b1);
04729 #endif
04730         break;
04731 
04732     case Q_UDP:
04733         b1 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_UDP, Q_IP, Q_DEFAULT);
04734 #ifdef INET6
04735         b0 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_UDP, Q_IPV6, Q_DEFAULT);
04736         gen_or(b0, b1);
04737 #endif
04738         break;
04739 
04740     case Q_ICMP:
04741         b1 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_ICMP, Q_IP, Q_DEFAULT);
04742         break;
04743 
04744 #ifndef IPPROTO_IGMP
04745 #define IPPROTO_IGMP    2
04746 #endif
04747 
04748     case Q_IGMP:
04749         b1 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_IGMP, Q_IP, Q_DEFAULT);
04750         break;
04751 
04752 #ifndef IPPROTO_IGRP
04753 #define IPPROTO_IGRP    9
04754 #endif
04755     case Q_IGRP:
04756         b1 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_IGRP, Q_IP, Q_DEFAULT);
04757         break;
04758 
04759 #ifndef IPPROTO_PIM
04760 #define IPPROTO_PIM 103
04761 #endif
04762 
04763     case Q_PIM:
04764         b1 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_PIM, Q_IP, Q_DEFAULT);
04765 #ifdef INET6
04766         b0 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_PIM, Q_IPV6, Q_DEFAULT);
04767         gen_or(b0, b1);
04768 #endif
04769         break;
04770 
04771 #ifndef IPPROTO_VRRP
04772 #define IPPROTO_VRRP    112
04773 #endif
04774 
04775     case Q_VRRP:
04776         b1 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_VRRP, Q_IP, Q_DEFAULT);
04777         break;
04778 
04779     case Q_IP:
04780         b1 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_IP);
04781         break;
04782 
04783     case Q_ARP:
04784         b1 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_ARP);
04785         break;
04786 
04787     case Q_RARP:
04788         b1 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_REVARP);
04789         break;
04790 
04791     case Q_LINK:
04792         bpf_error("link layer applied in wrong context");
04793 
04794     case Q_ATALK:
04795         b1 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_ATALK);
04796         break;
04797 
04798     case Q_AARP:
04799         b1 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_AARP);
04800         break;
04801 
04802     case Q_DECNET:
04803         b1 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_DN);
04804         break;
04805 
04806     case Q_SCA:
04807         b1 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_SCA);
04808         break;
04809 
04810     case Q_LAT:
04811         b1 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_LAT);
04812         break;
04813 
04814     case Q_MOPDL:
04815         b1 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_MOPDL);
04816         break;
04817 
04818     case Q_MOPRC:
04819         b1 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_MOPRC);
04820         break;
04821 
04822 #ifdef INET6
04823     case Q_IPV6:
04824         b1 = gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_IPV6);
04825         break;
04826 
04827 #ifndef IPPROTO_ICMPV6
04828 #define IPPROTO_ICMPV6  58
04829 #endif
04830     case Q_ICMPV6:
04831         b1 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_ICMPV6, Q_IPV6, Q_DEFAULT);
04832         break;
04833 #endif /* INET6 */
04834 
04835 #ifndef IPPROTO_AH
04836 #define IPPROTO_AH  51
04837 #endif
04838     case Q_AH:
04839         b1 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_AH, Q_IP, Q_DEFAULT);
04840 #ifdef INET6
04841         b0 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_AH, Q_IPV6, Q_DEFAULT);
04842         gen_or(b0, b1);
04843 #endif
04844         break;
04845 
04846 #ifndef IPPROTO_ESP
04847 #define IPPROTO_ESP 50
04848 #endif
04849     case Q_ESP:
04850         b1 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_ESP, Q_IP, Q_DEFAULT);
04851 #ifdef INET6
04852         b0 = gen_proto(IPPROTO_ESP, Q_IPV6, Q_DEFAULT);
04853         gen_or(b0, b1);
04854 #endif
04855         break;
04856 
04857     case Q_ISO:
04858         b1 = gen_linktype(LLCSAP_ISONS);
04859         break;
04860 
04861     case Q_ESIS:
04862         b1 = gen_proto(ISO9542_ESIS, Q_ISO, Q_DEFAULT);
04863         break;
04864 
04865     case Q_ISIS:
04866         b1 = gen_proto(ISO10589_ISIS, Q_ISO, Q_DEFAULT);
04867         break;
04868 
04869     case Q_ISIS_L1: /* all IS-IS Level1 PDU-Types */
04870         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L1_LAN_IIH, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04871         b1 = gen_proto(ISIS_PTP_IIH, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT); /* FIXME extract the circuit-type bits */
04872         gen_or(b0, b1);
04873         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L1_LSP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04874         gen_or(b0, b1);
04875         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L1_CSNP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04876         gen_or(b0, b1);
04877         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L1_PSNP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04878         gen_or(b0, b1);
04879         break;
04880 
04881     case Q_ISIS_L2: /* all IS-IS Level2 PDU-Types */
04882         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L2_LAN_IIH, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04883         b1 = gen_proto(ISIS_PTP_IIH, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT); /* FIXME extract the circuit-type bits */
04884         gen_or(b0, b1);
04885         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L2_LSP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04886         gen_or(b0, b1);
04887         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L2_CSNP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04888         gen_or(b0, b1);
04889         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L2_PSNP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04890         gen_or(b0, b1);
04891         break;
04892 
04893     case Q_ISIS_IIH: /* all IS-IS Hello PDU-Types */
04894         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L1_LAN_IIH, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04895         b1 = gen_proto(ISIS_L2_LAN_IIH, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04896         gen_or(b0, b1);
04897         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_PTP_IIH, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04898         gen_or(b0, b1);
04899         break;
04900 
04901     case Q_ISIS_LSP:
04902         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L1_LSP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04903         b1 = gen_proto(ISIS_L2_LSP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04904         gen_or(b0, b1);
04905         break;
04906 
04907     case Q_ISIS_SNP:
04908         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L1_CSNP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04909         b1 = gen_proto(ISIS_L2_CSNP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04910         gen_or(b0, b1);
04911         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L1_PSNP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04912         gen_or(b0, b1);
04913         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L2_PSNP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04914         gen_or(b0, b1);
04915         break;
04916 
04917     case Q_ISIS_CSNP:
04918         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L1_CSNP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04919         b1 = gen_proto(ISIS_L2_CSNP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04920         gen_or(b0, b1);
04921         break;
04922 
04923     case Q_ISIS_PSNP:
04924         b0 = gen_proto(ISIS_L1_PSNP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04925         b1 = gen_proto(ISIS_L2_PSNP, Q_ISIS, Q_DEFAULT);
04926         gen_or(b0, b1);
04927         break;
04928 
04929     case Q_CLNP:
04930         b1 = gen_proto(ISO8473_CLNP, Q_ISO, Q_DEFAULT);
04931         break;
04932 
04933     case Q_STP:
04934         b1 = gen_linktype(LLCSAP_8021D);
04935         break;
04936 
04937     case Q_IPX:
04938         b1 = gen_linktype(LLCSAP_IPX);
04939         break;
04940 
04941     case Q_NETBEUI:
04942         b1 = gen_linktype(LLCSAP_NETBEUI);
04943         break;
04944 
04945     case Q_RADIO:
04946         bpf_error("'radio' is not a valid protocol type");
04947 
04948     default:
04949         abort();
04950     }
04951     return b1;
04952 }
04953 
04954 static struct block *
04955 gen_ipfrag()
04956 {
04957     struct slist *s;
04958     struct block *b;
04959 
04960     /* not ip frag */
04961     s = gen_load_a(OR_NET, 6, BPF_H);
04962     b = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
04963     b->s.k = 0x1fff;
04964     b->stmts = s;
04965     gen_not(b);
04966 
04967     return b;
04968 }
04969 
04970 /*
04971  * Generate a comparison to a port value in the transport-layer header
04972  * at the specified offset from the beginning of that header.
04973  *
04974  * XXX - this handles a variable-length prefix preceding the link-layer
04975  * header, such as the radiotap or AVS radio prefix, but doesn't handle
04976  * variable-length link-layer headers (such as Token Ring or 802.11
04977  * headers).
04978  */
04979 static struct block *
04980 gen_portatom(off, v)
04981     int off;
04982     bpf_int32 v;
04983 {
04984     return gen_cmp(OR_TRAN_IPV4, off, BPF_H, v);
04985 }
04986 
04987 #ifdef INET6
04988 static struct block *
04989 gen_portatom6(off, v)
04990     int off;
04991     bpf_int32 v;
04992 {
04993     return gen_cmp(OR_TRAN_IPV6, off, BPF_H, v);
04994 }
04995 #endif/*INET6*/
04996 
04997 struct block *
04998 gen_portop(port, proto, dir)
04999     int port, proto, dir;
05000 {
05001     struct block *b0, *b1, *tmp;
05002 
05003     /* ip proto 'proto' */
05004     tmp = gen_cmp(OR_NET, 9, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)proto);
05005     b0 = gen_ipfrag();
05006     gen_and(tmp, b0);
05007 
05008     switch (dir) {
05009     case Q_SRC:
05010         b1 = gen_portatom(0, (bpf_int32)port);
05011         break;
05012 
05013     case Q_DST:
05014         b1 = gen_portatom(2, (bpf_int32)port);
05015         break;
05016 
05017     case Q_OR:
05018     case Q_DEFAULT:
05019         tmp = gen_portatom(0, (bpf_int32)port);
05020         b1 = gen_portatom(2, (bpf_int32)port);
05021         gen_or(tmp, b1);
05022         break;
05023 
05024     case Q_AND:
05025         tmp = gen_portatom(0, (bpf_int32)port);
05026         b1 = gen_portatom(2, (bpf_int32)port);
05027         gen_and(tmp, b1);
05028         break;
05029 
05030     default:
05031         abort();
05032     }
05033     gen_and(b0, b1);
05034 
05035     return b1;
05036 }
05037 
05038 static struct block *
05039 gen_port(port, ip_proto, dir)
05040     int port;
05041     int ip_proto;
05042     int dir;
05043 {
05044     struct block *b0, *b1, *tmp;
05045 
05046     /*
05047      * ether proto ip
05048      *
05049      * For FDDI, RFC 1188 says that SNAP encapsulation is used,
05050      * not LLC encapsulation with LLCSAP_IP.
05051      *
05052      * For IEEE 802 networks - which includes 802.5 token ring
05053      * (which is what DLT_IEEE802 means) and 802.11 - RFC 1042
05054      * says that SNAP encapsulation is used, not LLC encapsulation
05055      * with LLCSAP_IP.
05056      *
05057      * For LLC-encapsulated ATM/"Classical IP", RFC 1483 and
05058      * RFC 2225 say that SNAP encapsulation is used, not LLC
05059      * encapsulation with LLCSAP_IP.
05060      *
05061      * So we always check for ETHERTYPE_IP.
05062      */
05063     b0 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_IP);
05064 
05065     switch (ip_proto) {
05066     case IPPROTO_UDP:
05067     case IPPROTO_TCP:
05068     case IPPROTO_SCTP:
05069         b1 = gen_portop(port, ip_proto, dir);
05070         break;
05071 
05072     case PROTO_UNDEF:
05073         tmp = gen_portop(port, IPPROTO_TCP, dir);
05074         b1 = gen_portop(port, IPPROTO_UDP, dir);
05075         gen_or(tmp, b1);
05076         tmp = gen_portop(port, IPPROTO_SCTP, dir);
05077         gen_or(tmp, b1);
05078         break;
05079 
05080     default:
05081         abort();
05082     }
05083     gen_and(b0, b1);
05084     return b1;
05085 }
05086 
05087 #ifdef INET6
05088 struct block *
05089 gen_portop6(port, proto, dir)
05090     int port, proto, dir;
05091 {
05092     struct block *b0, *b1, *tmp;
05093 
05094     /* ip6 proto 'proto' */
05095     b0 = gen_cmp(OR_NET, 6, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)proto);
05096 
05097     switch (dir) {
05098     case Q_SRC:
05099         b1 = gen_portatom6(0, (bpf_int32)port);
05100         break;
05101 
05102     case Q_DST:
05103         b1 = gen_portatom6(2, (bpf_int32)port);
05104         break;
05105 
05106     case Q_OR:
05107     case Q_DEFAULT:
05108         tmp = gen_portatom6(0, (bpf_int32)port);
05109         b1 = gen_portatom6(2, (bpf_int32)port);
05110         gen_or(tmp, b1);
05111         break;
05112 
05113     case Q_AND:
05114         tmp = gen_portatom6(0, (bpf_int32)port);
05115         b1 = gen_portatom6(2, (bpf_int32)port);
05116         gen_and(tmp, b1);
05117         break;
05118 
05119     default:
05120         abort();
05121     }
05122     gen_and(b0, b1);
05123 
05124     return b1;
05125 }
05126 
05127 static struct block *
05128 gen_port6(port, ip_proto, dir)
05129     int port;
05130     int ip_proto;
05131     int dir;
05132 {
05133     struct block *b0, *b1, *tmp;
05134 
05135     /* link proto ip6 */
05136     b0 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_IPV6);
05137 
05138     switch (ip_proto) {
05139     case IPPROTO_UDP:
05140     case IPPROTO_TCP:
05141     case IPPROTO_SCTP:
05142         b1 = gen_portop6(port, ip_proto, dir);
05143         break;
05144 
05145     case PROTO_UNDEF:
05146         tmp = gen_portop6(port, IPPROTO_TCP, dir);
05147         b1 = gen_portop6(port, IPPROTO_UDP, dir);
05148         gen_or(tmp, b1);
05149         tmp = gen_portop6(port, IPPROTO_SCTP, dir);
05150         gen_or(tmp, b1);
05151         break;
05152 
05153     default:
05154         abort();
05155     }
05156     gen_and(b0, b1);
05157     return b1;
05158 }
05159 #endif /* INET6 */
05160 
05161 /* gen_portrange code */
05162 static struct block *
05163 gen_portrangeatom(off, v1, v2)
05164     int off;
05165     bpf_int32 v1, v2;
05166 {
05167     struct block *b1, *b2;
05168 
05169     if (v1 > v2) {
05170         /*
05171          * Reverse the order of the ports, so v1 is the lower one.
05172          */
05173         bpf_int32 vtemp;
05174 
05175         vtemp = v1;
05176         v1 = v2;
05177         v2 = vtemp;
05178     }
05179 
05180     b1 = gen_cmp_ge(OR_TRAN_IPV4, off, BPF_H, v1);
05181     b2 = gen_cmp_le(OR_TRAN_IPV4, off, BPF_H, v2);
05182 
05183     gen_and(b1, b2); 
05184 
05185     return b2;
05186 }
05187 
05188 struct block *
05189 gen_portrangeop(port1, port2, proto, dir)
05190     int port1, port2;
05191     int proto;
05192     int dir;
05193 {
05194     struct block *b0, *b1, *tmp;
05195 
05196     /* ip proto 'proto' */
05197     tmp = gen_cmp(OR_NET, 9, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)proto);
05198     b0 = gen_ipfrag();
05199     gen_and(tmp, b0);
05200 
05201     switch (dir) {
05202     case Q_SRC:
05203         b1 = gen_portrangeatom(0, (bpf_int32)port1, (bpf_int32)port2);
05204         break;
05205 
05206     case Q_DST:
05207         b1 = gen_portrangeatom(2, (bpf_int32)port1, (bpf_int32)port2);
05208         break;
05209 
05210     case Q_OR:
05211     case Q_DEFAULT:
05212         tmp = gen_portrangeatom(0, (bpf_int32)port1, (bpf_int32)port2);
05213         b1 = gen_portrangeatom(2, (bpf_int32)port1, (bpf_int32)port2);
05214         gen_or(tmp, b1);
05215         break;
05216 
05217     case Q_AND:
05218         tmp = gen_portrangeatom(0, (bpf_int32)port1, (bpf_int32)port2);
05219         b1 = gen_portrangeatom(2, (bpf_int32)port1, (bpf_int32)port2);
05220         gen_and(tmp, b1);
05221         break;
05222 
05223     default:
05224         abort();
05225     }
05226     gen_and(b0, b1);
05227 
05228     return b1;
05229 }
05230 
05231 static struct block *
05232 gen_portrange(port1, port2, ip_proto, dir)
05233     int port1, port2;
05234     int ip_proto;
05235     int dir;
05236 {
05237     struct block *b0, *b1, *tmp;
05238 
05239     /* link proto ip */
05240     b0 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_IP);
05241 
05242     switch (ip_proto) {
05243     case IPPROTO_UDP:
05244     case IPPROTO_TCP:
05245     case IPPROTO_SCTP:
05246         b1 = gen_portrangeop(port1, port2, ip_proto, dir);
05247         break;
05248 
05249     case PROTO_UNDEF:
05250         tmp = gen_portrangeop(port1, port2, IPPROTO_TCP, dir);
05251         b1 = gen_portrangeop(port1, port2, IPPROTO_UDP, dir);
05252         gen_or(tmp, b1);
05253         tmp = gen_portrangeop(port1, port2, IPPROTO_SCTP, dir);
05254         gen_or(tmp, b1);
05255         break;
05256 
05257     default:
05258         abort();
05259     }
05260     gen_and(b0, b1);
05261     return b1;
05262 }
05263 
05264 #ifdef INET6
05265 static struct block *
05266 gen_portrangeatom6(off, v1, v2)
05267     int off;
05268     bpf_int32 v1, v2;
05269 {
05270     struct block *b1, *b2;
05271 
05272     if (v1 > v2) {
05273         /*
05274          * Reverse the order of the ports, so v1 is the lower one.
05275          */
05276         bpf_int32 vtemp;
05277 
05278         vtemp = v1;
05279         v1 = v2;
05280         v2 = vtemp;
05281     }
05282 
05283     b1 = gen_cmp_ge(OR_TRAN_IPV6, off, BPF_H, v1);
05284     b2 = gen_cmp_le(OR_TRAN_IPV6, off, BPF_H, v2);
05285 
05286     gen_and(b1, b2); 
05287 
05288     return b2;
05289 }
05290 
05291 struct block *
05292 gen_portrangeop6(port1, port2, proto, dir)
05293     int port1, port2;
05294     int proto;
05295     int dir;
05296 {
05297     struct block *b0, *b1, *tmp;
05298 
05299     /* ip6 proto 'proto' */
05300     b0 = gen_cmp(OR_NET, 6, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)proto);
05301 
05302     switch (dir) {
05303     case Q_SRC:
05304         b1 = gen_portrangeatom6(0, (bpf_int32)port1, (bpf_int32)port2);
05305         break;
05306 
05307     case Q_DST:
05308         b1 = gen_portrangeatom6(2, (bpf_int32)port1, (bpf_int32)port2);
05309         break;
05310 
05311     case Q_OR:
05312     case Q_DEFAULT:
05313         tmp = gen_portrangeatom6(0, (bpf_int32)port1, (bpf_int32)port2);
05314         b1 = gen_portrangeatom6(2, (bpf_int32)port1, (bpf_int32)port2);
05315         gen_or(tmp, b1);
05316         break;
05317 
05318     case Q_AND:
05319         tmp = gen_portrangeatom6(0, (bpf_int32)port1, (bpf_int32)port2);
05320         b1 = gen_portrangeatom6(2, (bpf_int32)port1, (bpf_int32)port2);
05321         gen_and(tmp, b1);
05322         break;
05323 
05324     default:
05325         abort();
05326     }
05327     gen_and(b0, b1);
05328 
05329     return b1;
05330 }

05332 static struct block *

05334     int port1, port2;

05341     b0 =  gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_IPV6);
05342 
05343     switch (ip_proto) {
05344     case IPPROTO_UDP:
05345     case IPPROTO_TCP:
05346     case IPPROTO_SCTP:
05347         b1 = gen_portrangeop6(port1, port2, ip_proto, dir);
05348         break;
05349 
05350     case PROTO_UNDEF:
05351         tmp = gen_portrangeop6(port1, port2, IPPROTO_TCP, dir);
05352         b1 = gen_portrangeop6(port1, port2, IPPROTO_UDP, dir);
05353         gen_or(tmp, b1);
05354         tmp = gen_portrangeop6(port1, port2, IPPROTO_SCTP, dir);
05355         gen_or(tmp, b1);
05356         break;
05357 
05358     default:
05359         abort();
05360     }

05362     return b1;
05363 }
05364 #endif /* INET6 */
05365 
05366 static int
05367 lookup_proto(name, proto)
05368     register const char *name;
05369     register int proto;
05370 {
05371     register int v;
05372 
05373     switch (proto) {
05374 
05375     case Q_DEFAULT:
05376     case Q_IP:
05377     case Q_IPV6:
05378         v = pcap_nametoproto(name);
05379         if (v == PROTO_UNDEF)
05380             bpf_error("unknown ip proto '%s'", name);
05381         break;
05382 
05383     case Q_LINK:
05384         /* XXX should look up h/w protocol type based on linktype */
05385         v = pcap_nametoeproto(name);
05386         if (v == PROTO_UNDEF) {
05387             v = pcap_nametollc(name);
05388             if (v == PROTO_UNDEF)
05389                 bpf_error("unknown ether proto '%s'", name);
05390         }
05391         break;
05392 
05393     case Q_ISO:
05394         if (strcmp(name, "esis") == 0)
05395             v = ISO9542_ESIS;
05396         else if (strcmp(name, "isis") == 0)
05397             v = ISO10589_ISIS;
05398         else if (strcmp(name, "clnp") == 0)
05399             v = ISO8473_CLNP;
05400         else
05401             bpf_error("unknown osi proto '%s'", name);
05402         break;
05403 
05404     default:
05405         v = PROTO_UNDEF;
05406         break;
05407     }
05408     return v;
05409 }
