05411 #if 0
05412 struct stmt *
05413 gen_joinsp(s, n)
05414     struct stmt **s;
05415     int n;
05416 {
05417     return NULL;
05418 }
05419 #endif
05420 
05421 static struct block *
05422 gen_protochain(v, proto, dir)
05423     int v;
05424     int proto;
05425     int dir;
05426 {
05427 #ifdef NO_PROTOCHAIN
05428     return gen_proto(v, proto, dir);
05429 #else
05430     struct block *b0, *b;
05431     struct slist *s[100];
05432     int fix2, fix3, fix4, fix5;
05433     int ahcheck, again, end;
05434     int i, max;
05435     int reg2 = alloc_reg();
05436 
05437     memset(s, 0, sizeof(s));
05438     fix2 = fix3 = fix4 = fix5 = 0;
05439 
05440     switch (proto) {
05441     case Q_IP:
05442     case Q_IPV6:
05443         break;
05444     case Q_DEFAULT:
05445         b0 = gen_protochain(v, Q_IP, dir);
05446         b = gen_protochain(v, Q_IPV6, dir);
05447         gen_or(b0, b);
05448         return b;
05449     default:
05450         bpf_error("bad protocol applied for 'protochain'");
05451         /*NOTREACHED*/
05452     }
05453 
05454     /*
05455      * We don't handle variable-length prefixes before the link-layer
05456      * header, or variable-length link-layer headers, here yet.
05457      * We might want to add BPF instructions to do the protochain
05458      * work, to simplify that and, on platforms that have a BPF
05459      * interpreter with the new instructions, let the filtering
05460      * be done in the kernel.  (We already require a modified BPF
05461      * engine to do the protochain stuff, to support backward
05462      * branches, and backward branch support is unlikely to appear
05463      * in kernel BPF engines.)
05464      */
05465     switch (linktype) {
05466 
05467     case DLT_IEEE802_11:
05468     case DLT_PRISM_HEADER:
05469     case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO_AVS:
05470     case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO:
05471     case DLT_PPI:
05472         bpf_error("'protochain' not supported with 802.11");
05473     }
05474 
05475     no_optimize = 1; /*this code is not compatible with optimzer yet */
05476 
05477     /*
05478      * s[0] is a dummy entry to protect other BPF insn from damage
05479      * by s[fix] = foo with uninitialized variable "fix".  It is somewhat
05480      * hard to find interdependency made by jump table fixup.
05481      */
05482     i = 0;
05483     s[i] = new_stmt(0); /*dummy*/
05484     i++;
05485 
05486     switch (proto) {
05487     case Q_IP:
05488         b0 = gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_IP);
05489 
05490         /* A = ip->ip_p */
05491         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_ABS|BPF_B);
05492         s[i]->s.k = off_macpl + off_nl + 9;
05493         i++;
05494         /* X = ip->ip_hl << 2 */
05495         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_LDX|BPF_MSH|BPF_B);
05496         s[i]->s.k = off_macpl + off_nl;
05497         i++;
05498         break;
05499 #ifdef INET6
05500     case Q_IPV6:
05501         b0 = gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_IPV6);
05502 
05503         /* A = ip6->ip_nxt */
05504         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_ABS|BPF_B);
05505         s[i]->s.k = off_macpl + off_nl + 6;
05506         i++;
05507         /* X = sizeof(struct ip6_hdr) */
05508         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_LDX|BPF_IMM);
05509         s[i]->s.k = 40;
05510         i++;
05511         break;
05512 #endif
05513     default:
05514         bpf_error("unsupported proto to gen_protochain");
05515         /*NOTREACHED*/
05516     }
05517 
05518     /* again: if (A == v) goto end; else fall through; */
05519     again = i;
05520     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_JMP|BPF_JEQ|BPF_K);
05521     s[i]->s.k = v;
05522     s[i]->s.jt = NULL;      /*later*/
05523     s[i]->s.jf = NULL;      /*update in next stmt*/
05524     fix5 = i;
05525     i++;
05526 
05527 #ifndef IPPROTO_NONE
05528 #define IPPROTO_NONE    59
05529 #endif
05530     /* if (A == IPPROTO_NONE) goto end */
05531     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_JMP|BPF_JEQ|BPF_K);
05532     s[i]->s.jt = NULL;  /*later*/
05533     s[i]->s.jf = NULL;  /*update in next stmt*/
05534     s[i]->s.k = IPPROTO_NONE;
05535     s[fix5]->s.jf = s[i];
05536     fix2 = i;
05537     i++;
05538 
05539 #ifdef INET6
05540     if (proto == Q_IPV6) {
05541         int v6start, v6end, v6advance, j;
05542 
05543         v6start = i;
05544         /* if (A == IPPROTO_HOPOPTS) goto v6advance */
05545         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_JMP|BPF_JEQ|BPF_K);
05546         s[i]->s.jt = NULL;  /*later*/
05547         s[i]->s.jf = NULL;  /*update in next stmt*/
05548         s[i]->s.k = IPPROTO_HOPOPTS;
05549         s[fix2]->s.jf = s[i];
05550         i++;
05551         /* if (A == IPPROTO_DSTOPTS) goto v6advance */
05552         s[i - 1]->s.jf = s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_JMP|BPF_JEQ|BPF_K);
05553         s[i]->s.jt = NULL;  /*later*/
05554         s[i]->s.jf = NULL;  /*update in next stmt*/
05555         s[i]->s.k = IPPROTO_DSTOPTS;
05556         i++;
05557         /* if (A == IPPROTO_ROUTING) goto v6advance */
05558         s[i - 1]->s.jf = s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_JMP|BPF_JEQ|BPF_K);
05559         s[i]->s.jt = NULL;  /*later*/
05560         s[i]->s.jf = NULL;  /*update in next stmt*/
05561         s[i]->s.k = IPPROTO_ROUTING;
05562         i++;
05563         /* if (A == IPPROTO_FRAGMENT) goto v6advance; else goto ahcheck; */
05564         s[i - 1]->s.jf = s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_JMP|BPF_JEQ|BPF_K);
05565         s[i]->s.jt = NULL;  /*later*/
05566         s[i]->s.jf = NULL;  /*later*/
05567         s[i]->s.k = IPPROTO_FRAGMENT;
05568         fix3 = i;
05569         v6end = i;
05570         i++;
05571 
05572         /* v6advance: */
05573         v6advance = i;
05574 
05575         /*
05576          * in short,
05577          * A = P[X];
05578          * X = X + (P[X + 1] + 1) * 8;
05579          */
05580         /* A = X */
05581         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_MISC|BPF_TXA);
05582         i++;
05583         /* A = P[X + packet head] */
05584         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_IND|BPF_B);
05585         s[i]->s.k = off_macpl + off_nl;
05586         i++;
05587         /* MEM[reg2] = A */
05588         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_ST);
05589         s[i]->s.k = reg2;
05590         i++;
05591         /* A = X */
05592         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_MISC|BPF_TXA);
05593         i++;
05594         /* A += 1 */
05595         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_ADD|BPF_K);
05596         s[i]->s.k = 1;
05597         i++;
05598         /* X = A */
05599         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_MISC|BPF_TAX);
05600         i++;
05601         /* A = P[X + packet head]; */
05602         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_IND|BPF_B);
05603         s[i]->s.k = off_macpl + off_nl;
05604         i++;
05605         /* A += 1 */
05606         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_ADD|BPF_K);
05607         s[i]->s.k = 1;
05608         i++;
05609         /* A *= 8 */
05610         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_MUL|BPF_K);
05611         s[i]->s.k = 8;
05612         i++;
05613         /* X = A; */
05614         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_MISC|BPF_TAX);
05615         i++;
05616         /* A = MEM[reg2] */
05617         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_MEM);
05618         s[i]->s.k = reg2;
05619         i++;
05620 
05621         /* goto again; (must use BPF_JA for backward jump) */
05622         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_JMP|BPF_JA);
05623         s[i]->s.k = again - i - 1;
05624         s[i - 1]->s.jf = s[i];
05625         i++;
05626 
05627         /* fixup */
05628         for (j = v6start; j <= v6end; j++)
05629             s[j]->s.jt = s[v6advance];
05630     } else
05631 #endif
05632     {
05633         /* nop */
05634         s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_ADD|BPF_K);
05635         s[i]->s.k = 0;
05636         s[fix2]->s.jf = s[i];
05637         i++;
05638     }
05639 
05640     /* ahcheck: */
05641     ahcheck = i;
05642     /* if (A == IPPROTO_AH) then fall through; else goto end; */
05643     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_JMP|BPF_JEQ|BPF_K);
05644     s[i]->s.jt = NULL;  /*later*/
05645     s[i]->s.jf = NULL;  /*later*/
05646     s[i]->s.k = IPPROTO_AH;
05647     if (fix3)
05648         s[fix3]->s.jf = s[ahcheck];
05649     fix4 = i;
05650     i++;
05651 
05652     /*
05653      * in short,
05654      * A = P[X];
05655      * X = X + (P[X + 1] + 2) * 4;
05656      */
05657     /* A = X */
05658     s[i - 1]->s.jt = s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_MISC|BPF_TXA);
05659     i++;
05660     /* A = P[X + packet head]; */
05661     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_IND|BPF_B);
05662     s[i]->s.k = off_macpl + off_nl;
05663     i++;
05664     /* MEM[reg2] = A */
05665     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_ST);
05666     s[i]->s.k = reg2;
05667     i++;
05668     /* A = X */
05669     s[i - 1]->s.jt = s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_MISC|BPF_TXA);
05670     i++;
05671     /* A += 1 */
05672     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_ADD|BPF_K);
05673     s[i]->s.k = 1;
05674     i++;
05675     /* X = A */
05676     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_MISC|BPF_TAX);
05677     i++;
05678     /* A = P[X + packet head] */
05679     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_IND|BPF_B);
05680     s[i]->s.k = off_macpl + off_nl;
05681     i++;
05682     /* A += 2 */
05683     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_ADD|BPF_K);
05684     s[i]->s.k = 2;
05685     i++;
05686     /* A *= 4 */
05687     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_MUL|BPF_K);
05688     s[i]->s.k = 4;
05689     i++;
05690     /* X = A; */
05691     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_MISC|BPF_TAX);
05692     i++;
05693     /* A = MEM[reg2] */
05694     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_MEM);
05695     s[i]->s.k = reg2;
05696     i++;
05697 
05698     /* goto again; (must use BPF_JA for backward jump) */
05699     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_JMP|BPF_JA);
05700     s[i]->s.k = again - i - 1;
05701     i++;
05702 
05703     /* end: nop */
05704     end = i;
05705     s[i] = new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_ADD|BPF_K);
05706     s[i]->s.k = 0;
05707     s[fix2]->s.jt = s[end];
05708     s[fix4]->s.jf = s[end];
05709     s[fix5]->s.jt = s[end];
05710     i++;
05711 
05712     /*
05713      * make slist chain
05714      */
05715     max = i;
05716     for (i = 0; i < max - 1; i++)
05717         s[i]->next = s[i + 1];
05718     s[max - 1]->next = NULL;
05719 
05720     /*
05721      * emit final check
05722      */
05723     b = new_block(JMP(BPF_JEQ));
05724     b->stmts = s[1];    /*remember, s[0] is dummy*/
05725     b->s.k = v;
05726 
05727     free_reg(reg2);
05728 
05729     gen_and(b0, b);
05730     return b;
05731 #endif
05732 }
05733 
05734 static struct block *
05735 gen_check_802_11_data_frame()
05736 {
05737     struct slist *s;
05738     struct block *b0, *b1;
05739 
05740     /*
05741      * A data frame has the 0x08 bit (b3) in the frame control field set
05742      * and the 0x04 bit (b2) clear.
05743      */
05744     s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B);
05745     b0 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
05746     b0->s.k = 0x08;
05747     b0->stmts = s;
05748     
05749     s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B);
05750     b1 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
05751     b1->s.k = 0x04;
05752     b1->stmts = s;
05753     gen_not(b1);
05754 
05755     gen_and(b1, b0);
05756 
05757     return b0;
05758 }
05759 
05760 /*
05761  * Generate code that checks whether the packet is a packet for protocol
05762  * <proto> and whether the type field in that protocol's header has
05763  * the value <v>, e.g. if <proto> is Q_IP, it checks whether it's an
05764  * IP packet and checks the protocol number in the IP header against <v>.
05765  *
05766  * If <proto> is Q_DEFAULT, i.e. just "proto" was specified, it checks
05767  * against Q_IP and Q_IPV6.
05768  */
05769 static struct block *
05770 gen_proto(v, proto, dir)
05771     int v;
05772     int proto;
05773     int dir;
05774 {
05775     struct block *b0, *b1;
05776 
05777     if (dir != Q_DEFAULT)
05778         bpf_error("direction applied to 'proto'");
05779 
05780     switch (proto) {
05781     case Q_DEFAULT:
05782 #ifdef INET6
05783         b0 = gen_proto(v, Q_IP, dir);
05784         b1 = gen_proto(v, Q_IPV6, dir);
05785         gen_or(b0, b1);
05786         return b1;
05787 #else
05788         /*FALLTHROUGH*/
05789 #endif
05790     case Q_IP:
05791         /*
05792          * For FDDI, RFC 1188 says that SNAP encapsulation is used,
05793          * not LLC encapsulation with LLCSAP_IP.
05794          *
05795          * For IEEE 802 networks - which includes 802.5 token ring
05796          * (which is what DLT_IEEE802 means) and 802.11 - RFC 1042
05797          * says that SNAP encapsulation is used, not LLC encapsulation
05798          * with LLCSAP_IP.
05799          *
05800          * For LLC-encapsulated ATM/"Classical IP", RFC 1483 and
05801          * RFC 2225 say that SNAP encapsulation is used, not LLC
05802          * encapsulation with LLCSAP_IP.
05803          *
05804          * So we always check for ETHERTYPE_IP.
05805          */
05806         b0 = gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_IP);
05807 #ifndef CHASE_CHAIN
05808         b1 = gen_cmp(OR_NET, 9, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)v);
05809 #else
05810         b1 = gen_protochain(v, Q_IP);
05811 #endif
05812         gen_and(b0, b1);
05813         return b1;
05814 
05815     case Q_ISO:
05816         switch (linktype) {
05817 
05818         case DLT_FRELAY:
05819             /*
05820              * Frame Relay packets typically have an OSI
05821              * NLPID at the beginning; "gen_linktype(LLCSAP_ISONS)"
05822              * generates code to check for all the OSI
05823              * NLPIDs, so calling it and then adding a check
05824              * for the particular NLPID for which we're
05825              * looking is bogus, as we can just check for
05826              * the NLPID.
05827              *
05828              * What we check for is the NLPID and a frame
05829              * control field value of UI, i.e. 0x03 followed
05830              * by the NLPID.
05831              *
05832              * XXX - assumes a 2-byte Frame Relay header with
05833              * DLCI and flags.  What if the address is longer?
05834              *
05835              * XXX - what about SNAP-encapsulated frames?
05836              */
05837             return gen_cmp(OR_LINK, 2, BPF_H, (0x03<<8) | v);
05838             /*NOTREACHED*/
05839             break;
05840 
05841         case DLT_C_HDLC:
05842             /*
05843              * Cisco uses an Ethertype lookalike - for OSI,
05844              * it's 0xfefe.
05845              */
05846             b0 = gen_linktype(LLCSAP_ISONS<<8 | LLCSAP_ISONS);
05847             /* OSI in C-HDLC is stuffed with a fudge byte */
05848             b1 = gen_cmp(OR_NET_NOSNAP, 1, BPF_B, (long)v);
05849             gen_and(b0, b1);
05850             return b1;
05851 
05852         default:
05853             b0 = gen_linktype(LLCSAP_ISONS);
05854             b1 = gen_cmp(OR_NET_NOSNAP, 0, BPF_B, (long)v);
05855             gen_and(b0, b1);
05856             return b1;
05857         }
05858 
05859     case Q_ISIS:
05860         b0 = gen_proto(ISO10589_ISIS, Q_ISO, Q_DEFAULT);
05861         /*
05862          * 4 is the offset of the PDU type relative to the IS-IS
05863          * header.
05864          */
05865         b1 = gen_cmp(OR_NET_NOSNAP, 4, BPF_B, (long)v);
05866         gen_and(b0, b1);
05867         return b1;
05868 
05869     case Q_ARP:
05870         bpf_error("arp does not encapsulate another protocol");
05871         /* NOTREACHED */
05872 
05873     case Q_RARP:
05874         bpf_error("rarp does not encapsulate another protocol");
05875         /* NOTREACHED */
05876 
05877     case Q_ATALK:
05878         bpf_error("atalk encapsulation is not specifiable");
05879         /* NOTREACHED */
05880 
05881     case Q_DECNET:
05882         bpf_error("decnet encapsulation is not specifiable");
05883         /* NOTREACHED */
05884 
05885     case Q_SCA:
05886         bpf_error("sca does not encapsulate another protocol");
05887         /* NOTREACHED */
05888 
05889     case Q_LAT:
05890         bpf_error("lat does not encapsulate another protocol");
05891         /* NOTREACHED */
05892 
05893     case Q_MOPRC:
05894         bpf_error("moprc does not encapsulate another protocol");
05895         /* NOTREACHED */
05896 
05897     case Q_MOPDL:
05898         bpf_error("mopdl does not encapsulate another protocol");
05899         /* NOTREACHED */
05900 
05901     case Q_LINK:
05902         return gen_linktype(v);
05903 
05904     case Q_UDP:
05905         bpf_error("'udp proto' is bogus");
05906         /* NOTREACHED */
05907 
05908     case Q_TCP:
05909         bpf_error("'tcp proto' is bogus");
05910         /* NOTREACHED */
05911 
05912     case Q_SCTP:
05913         bpf_error("'sctp proto' is bogus");
05914         /* NOTREACHED */
05915 
05916     case Q_ICMP:
05917         bpf_error("'icmp proto' is bogus");
05918         /* NOTREACHED */
05919 
05920     case Q_IGMP:
05921         bpf_error("'igmp proto' is bogus");
05922         /* NOTREACHED */
05923 
05924     case Q_IGRP:
05925         bpf_error("'igrp proto' is bogus");
05926         /* NOTREACHED */
05927 
05928     case Q_PIM:
05929         bpf_error("'pim proto' is bogus");
05930         /* NOTREACHED */
05931 
05932     case Q_VRRP:
05933         bpf_error("'vrrp proto' is bogus");
05934         /* NOTREACHED */
05935 
05936 #ifdef INET6
05937     case Q_IPV6:
05938         b0 = gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_IPV6);
05939 #ifndef CHASE_CHAIN
05940         b1 = gen_cmp(OR_NET, 6, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)v);
05941 #else
05942         b1 = gen_protochain(v, Q_IPV6);
05943 #endif
05944         gen_and(b0, b1);
05945         return b1;
05946 
05947     case Q_ICMPV6:
05948         bpf_error("'icmp6 proto' is bogus");
05949 #endif /* INET6 */
05950 
05951     case Q_AH:
05952         bpf_error("'ah proto' is bogus");
05953 
05954     case Q_ESP:
05955         bpf_error("'ah proto' is bogus");
05956 
05957     case Q_STP:
05958         bpf_error("'stp proto' is bogus");
05959 
05960     case Q_IPX:
05961         bpf_error("'ipx proto' is bogus");
05962 
05963     case Q_NETBEUI:
05964         bpf_error("'netbeui proto' is bogus");
05965 
05966     case Q_RADIO:
05967         bpf_error("'radio proto' is bogus");
05968 
05969     default:
05970         abort();
05971         /* NOTREACHED */
05972     }
05973     /* NOTREACHED */
05974 }
05975 
05976 struct block *
05977 gen_scode(name, q)
05978     register const char *name;
05979     struct qual q;
05980 {
05981     int proto = q.proto;
05982     int dir = q.dir;
05983     int tproto;
05984     u_char *eaddr;
05985     bpf_u_int32 mask, addr;
05986 #ifndef INET6
05987     bpf_u_int32 **alist;
05988 #else
05989     int tproto6;
05990     struct sockaddr_in *sin4;
05991     struct sockaddr_in6 *sin6;
05992     struct addrinfo *res, *res0;
05993     struct in6_addr mask128;
05994 #endif /*INET6*/
05995     struct block *b, *tmp;
05996     int port, real_proto;
05997     int port1, port2;
05998 
05999     switch (q.addr) {
06000 
06001     case Q_NET:
06002         addr = pcap_nametonetaddr(name);
06003         if (addr == 0)
06004             bpf_error("unknown network '%s'", name);
06005         /* Left justify network addr and calculate its network mask */
06006         mask = 0xffffffff;
06007         while (addr && (addr & 0xff000000) == 0) {
06008             addr <<= 8;
06009             mask <<= 8;
06010         }
06011         return gen_host(addr, mask, proto, dir, q.addr);
06012 
06013     case Q_DEFAULT:
06014     case Q_HOST:
06015         if (proto == Q_LINK) {
06016             switch (linktype) {
06017 
06018             case DLT_EN10MB:
06019                 eaddr = pcap_ether_hostton(name);
06020                 if (eaddr == NULL)
06021                     bpf_error(
06022                         "unknown ether host '%s'", name);
06023                 b = gen_ehostop(eaddr, dir);
06024                 free(eaddr);
06025                 return b;
06026 
06027             case DLT_FDDI:
06028                 eaddr = pcap_ether_hostton(name);
06029                 if (eaddr == NULL)
06030                     bpf_error(
06031                         "unknown FDDI host '%s'", name);
06032                 b = gen_fhostop(eaddr, dir);
06033                 free(eaddr);
06034                 return b;
06035 
06036             case DLT_IEEE802:
06037                 eaddr = pcap_ether_hostton(name);
06038                 if (eaddr == NULL)
06039                     bpf_error(
06040                         "unknown token ring host '%s'", name);
06041                 b = gen_thostop(eaddr, dir);
06042                 free(eaddr);
06043                 return b;
06044 
06045             case DLT_IEEE802_11:
06046             case DLT_PRISM_HEADER:
06047             case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO_AVS:
06048             case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO:
06049             case DLT_PPI:
06050                 eaddr = pcap_ether_hostton(name);
06051                 if (eaddr == NULL)
06052                     bpf_error(
06053                         "unknown 802.11 host '%s'", name);
06054                 b = gen_wlanhostop(eaddr, dir);
06055                 free(eaddr);
06056                 return b;
06057 
06058             case DLT_IP_OVER_FC:
06059                 eaddr = pcap_ether_hostton(name);
06060                 if (eaddr == NULL)
06061                     bpf_error(
06062                         "unknown Fibre Channel host '%s'", name);
06063                 b = gen_ipfchostop(eaddr, dir);
06064                 free(eaddr);
06065                 return b;
06066 
06067             case DLT_SUNATM:
06068                 if (!is_lane)
06069                     break;
06070 
06071                 /*
06072                  * Check that the packet doesn't begin
06073                  * with an LE Control marker.  (We've
06074                  * already generated a test for LANE.)
06075                  */
06076                 tmp = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, SUNATM_PKT_BEGIN_POS,
06077                     BPF_H, 0xFF00);
06078                 gen_not(tmp);
06079 
06080                 eaddr = pcap_ether_hostton(name);
06081                 if (eaddr == NULL)
06082                     bpf_error(
06083                         "unknown ether host '%s'", name);
06084                 b = gen_ehostop(eaddr, dir);
06085                 gen_and(tmp, b);
06086                 free(eaddr);
06087                 return b;
06088             }
06089 
06090             bpf_error("only ethernet/FDDI/token ring/802.11/ATM LANE/Fibre Channel supports link-level host name");
06091         } else if (proto == Q_DECNET) {
06092             unsigned short dn_addr = __pcap_nametodnaddr(name);
06093             /*
06094              * I don't think DECNET hosts can be multihomed, so
06095              * there is no need to build up a list of addresses
06096              */
06097             return (gen_host(dn_addr, 0, proto, dir, q.addr));
06098         } else {
06099 #ifndef INET6
06100             alist = pcap_nametoaddr(name);
06101             if (alist == NULL || *alist == NULL)
06102                 bpf_error("unknown host '%s'", name);
06103             tproto = proto;
06104             if (off_linktype == (u_int)-1 && tproto == Q_DEFAULT)
06105                 tproto = Q_IP;
06106             b = gen_host(**alist++, 0xffffffff, tproto, dir, q.addr);
06107             while (*alist) {
06108                 tmp = gen_host(**alist++, 0xffffffff,
06109                            tproto, dir, q.addr);
06110                 gen_or(b, tmp);
06111                 b = tmp;
06112             }
06113             return b;
06114 #else
06115             memset(&mask128, 0xff, sizeof(mask128));
06116             res0 = res = pcap_nametoaddrinfo(name);
06117             if (res == NULL)
06118                 bpf_error("unknown host '%s'", name);
06119             ai = res;
06120             b = tmp = NULL;
06121             tproto = tproto6 = proto;
06122             if (off_linktype == -1 && tproto == Q_DEFAULT) {
06123                 tproto = Q_IP;
06124                 tproto6 = Q_IPV6;
06125             }
06126             for (res = res0; res; res = res->ai_next) {
06127                 switch (res->ai_family) {
06128                 case AF_INET:
06129                     if (tproto == Q_IPV6)
06130                         continue;
06131 
06132                     sin4 = (struct sockaddr_in *)
06133                         res->ai_addr;
06134                     tmp = gen_host(ntohl(sin4->sin_addr.s_addr),
06135                         0xffffffff, tproto, dir, q.addr);
06136                     break;
06137                 case AF_INET6:
06138                     if (tproto6 == Q_IP)
06139                         continue;
06140 
06141                     sin6 = (struct sockaddr_in6 *)
06142                         res->ai_addr;
06143                     tmp = gen_host6(&sin6->sin6_addr,
06144                         &mask128, tproto6, dir, q.addr);
06145                     break;
06146                 default:
06147                     continue;
06148                 }
06149                 if (b)
06150                     gen_or(b, tmp);
06151                 b = tmp;
06152             }
06153             ai = NULL;
06154             freeaddrinfo(res0);
06155             if (b == NULL) {
06156                 bpf_error("unknown host '%s'%s", name,
06157                     (proto == Q_DEFAULT)
06158                     ? ""
06159                     : " for specified address family");
06160             }
06161             return b;
06162 #endif /*INET6*/
06163         }
06164 
06165     case Q_PORT:
06166         if (proto != Q_DEFAULT &&
06167             proto != Q_UDP && proto != Q_TCP && proto != Q_SCTP)
06168             bpf_error("illegal qualifier of 'port'");
06169         if (pcap_nametoport(name, &port, &real_proto) == 0)
06170             bpf_error("unknown port '%s'", name);
06171         if (proto == Q_UDP) {
06172             if (real_proto == IPPROTO_TCP)
06173                 bpf_error("port '%s' is tcp", name);
06174             else if (real_proto == IPPROTO_SCTP)
06175                 bpf_error("port '%s' is sctp", name);
06176             else
06177                 /* override PROTO_UNDEF */
06178                 real_proto = IPPROTO_UDP;
06179         }
06180         if (proto == Q_TCP) {
06181             if (real_proto == IPPROTO_UDP)
06182                 bpf_error("port '%s' is udp", name);
06183 
06184             else if (real_proto == IPPROTO_SCTP)
06185                 bpf_error("port '%s' is sctp", name);
06186             else
06187                 /* override PROTO_UNDEF */
06188                 real_proto = IPPROTO_TCP;
06189         }
06190         if (proto == Q_SCTP) {
06191             if (real_proto == IPPROTO_UDP)
06192                 bpf_error("port '%s' is udp", name);
06193 
06194             else if (real_proto == IPPROTO_TCP)
06195                 bpf_error("port '%s' is tcp", name);
06196             else
06197                 /* override PROTO_UNDEF */
06198                 real_proto = IPPROTO_SCTP;
06199         }
06200 #ifndef INET6
06201         return gen_port(port, real_proto, dir);
06202 #else
06203         b = gen_port(port, real_proto, dir);
06204         gen_or(gen_port6(port, real_proto, dir), b);
06205         return b;
06206 #endif /* INET6 */
06207 
06208     case Q_PORTRANGE:
06209         if (proto != Q_DEFAULT &&
06210             proto != Q_UDP && proto != Q_TCP && proto != Q_SCTP)
06211             bpf_error("illegal qualifier of 'portrange'");
06212         if (pcap_nametoportrange(name, &port1, &port2, &real_proto) == 0) 
06213             bpf_error("unknown port in range '%s'", name);
06214         if (proto == Q_UDP) {
06215             if (real_proto == IPPROTO_TCP)
06216                 bpf_error("port in range '%s' is tcp", name);
06217             else if (real_proto == IPPROTO_SCTP)
06218                 bpf_error("port in range '%s' is sctp", name);
06219             else
06220                 /* override PROTO_UNDEF */
06221                 real_proto = IPPROTO_UDP;
06222         }
06223         if (proto == Q_TCP) {
06224             if (real_proto == IPPROTO_UDP)
06225                 bpf_error("port in range '%s' is udp", name);
06226             else if (real_proto == IPPROTO_SCTP)
06227                 bpf_error("port in range '%s' is sctp", name);
06228             else
06229                 /* override PROTO_UNDEF */
06230                 real_proto = IPPROTO_TCP;
06231         }
06232         if (proto == Q_SCTP) {
06233             if (real_proto == IPPROTO_UDP)
06234                 bpf_error("port in range '%s' is udp", name);
06235             else if (real_proto == IPPROTO_TCP)
06236                 bpf_error("port in range '%s' is tcp", name);
06237             else
06238                 /* override PROTO_UNDEF */
06239                 real_proto = IPPROTO_SCTP;  
06240         }
06241 #ifndef INET6
06242         return gen_portrange(port1, port2, real_proto, dir);
06243 #else
06244         b = gen_portrange(port1, port2, real_proto, dir);
06245         gen_or(gen_portrange6(port1, port2, real_proto, dir), b);
06246         return b;
06247 #endif /* INET6 */
06248 
06249     case Q_GATEWAY:
06250 #ifndef INET6
06251         eaddr = pcap_ether_hostton(name);
06252         if (eaddr == NULL)
06253             bpf_error("unknown ether host: %s", name);
06254 
06255         alist = pcap_nametoaddr(name);
06256         if (alist == NULL || *alist == NULL)
06257             bpf_error("unknown host '%s'", name);
06258         b = gen_gateway(eaddr, alist, proto, dir);
06259         free(eaddr);
06260         return b;
06261 #else
06262         bpf_error("'gateway' not supported in this configuration");
06263 #endif /*INET6*/
06264 
06265     case Q_PROTO:
06266         real_proto = lookup_proto(name, proto);
06267         if (real_proto >= 0)
06268             return gen_proto(real_proto, proto, dir);
06269         else
06270             bpf_error("unknown protocol: %s", name);
06271 
06272     case Q_PROTOCHAIN:
06273         real_proto = lookup_proto(name, proto);
06274         if (real_proto >= 0)
06275             return gen_protochain(real_proto, proto, dir);
06276         else
06277             bpf_error("unknown protocol: %s", name);
06278 
06279     case Q_UNDEF:
06280         syntax();
06281         /* NOTREACHED */
06282     }
06283     abort();
06284     /* NOTREACHED */
06285 }
06286 
06287 struct block *
06288 gen_mcode(s1, s2, masklen, q)
06289     register const char *s1, *s2;
06290     register int masklen;
06291     struct qual q;
06292 {
06293     register int nlen, mlen;
06294     bpf_u_int32 n, m;
06295 
06296     nlen = __pcap_atoin(s1, &n);
06297     /* Promote short ipaddr */
06298     n <<= 32 - nlen;
06299 
06300     if (s2 != NULL) {
06301         mlen = __pcap_atoin(s2, &m);
06302         /* Promote short ipaddr */
06303         m <<= 32 - mlen;
06304         if ((n & ~m) != 0)
06305             bpf_error("non-network bits set in \"%s mask %s\"",
06306                 s1, s2);
06307     } else {
06308         /* Convert mask len to mask */
06309         if (masklen > 32)
06310             bpf_error("mask length must be <= 32");
06311         if (masklen == 0) {
06312             /*
06313              * X << 32 is not guaranteed by C to be 0; it's
06314              * undefined.
06315              */
06316             m = 0;
06317         } else
06318             m = 0xffffffff << (32 - masklen);
06319         if ((n & ~m) != 0)
06320             bpf_error("non-network bits set in \"%s/%d\"",
06321                 s1, masklen);
06322     }
06323 
06324     switch (q.addr) {
06325 
06326     case Q_NET:
06327         return gen_host(n, m, q.proto, q.dir, q.addr);
06328 
06329     default:
06330         bpf_error("Mask syntax for networks only");
06331         /* NOTREACHED */
06332     }
06333     /* NOTREACHED */
06334     return NULL;
06335 }
06336 
06337 struct block *
06338 gen_ncode(s, v, q)
06339     register const char *s;
06340     bpf_u_int32 v;
06341     struct qual q;
06342 {
06343     bpf_u_int32 mask;
06344     int proto = q.proto;
06345     int dir = q.dir;
06346     register int vlen;
06347 
06348     if (s == NULL)
06349         vlen = 32;
06350     else if (q.proto == Q_DECNET)
06351         vlen = __pcap_atodn(s, &v);
06352     else
06353         vlen = __pcap_atoin(s, &v);
06354 
06355     switch (q.addr) {
06356 
06357     case Q_DEFAULT:
06358     case Q_HOST:
06359     case Q_NET:
06360         if (proto == Q_DECNET)
06361             return gen_host(v, 0, proto, dir, q.addr);
06362         else if (proto == Q_LINK) {
06363             bpf_error("illegal link layer address");
06364         } else {
06365             mask = 0xffffffff;
06366             if (s == NULL && q.addr == Q_NET) {
06367                 /* Promote short net number */
06368                 while (v && (v & 0xff000000) == 0) {
06369                     v <<= 8;
06370                     mask <<= 8;
06371                 }
06372             } else {
06373                 /* Promote short ipaddr */
06374                 v <<= 32 - vlen;
06375                 mask <<= 32 - vlen;
06376             }
06377             return gen_host(v, mask, proto, dir, q.addr);
06378         }
06379 
06380     case Q_PORT:
06381         if (proto == Q_UDP)
06382             proto = IPPROTO_UDP;
06383         else if (proto == Q_TCP)
06384             proto = IPPROTO_TCP;
06385         else if (proto == Q_SCTP)
06386             proto = IPPROTO_SCTP;
06387         else if (proto == Q_DEFAULT)
06388             proto = PROTO_UNDEF;
06389         else
06390             bpf_error("illegal qualifier of 'port'");
06391 
06392 #ifndef INET6
06393         return gen_port((int)v, proto, dir);
06394 #else
06395         {
06396         struct block *b;
06397         b = gen_port((int)v, proto, dir);
06398         gen_or(gen_port6((int)v, proto, dir), b);
06399         return b;
06400         }
06401 #endif /* INET6 */
06402 
06403     case Q_PORTRANGE:
06404         if (proto == Q_UDP)
06405             proto = IPPROTO_UDP;
06406         else if (proto == Q_TCP)
06407             proto = IPPROTO_TCP;
06408         else if (proto == Q_SCTP)
06409             proto = IPPROTO_SCTP;
06410         else if (proto == Q_DEFAULT)
06411             proto = PROTO_UNDEF;
06412         else
06413             bpf_error("illegal qualifier of 'portrange'");
06414 
06415 #ifndef INET6
06416         return gen_portrange((int)v, (int)v, proto, dir);
06417 #else
06418         {
06419         struct block *b;
06420         b = gen_portrange((int)v, (int)v, proto, dir);
06421         gen_or(gen_portrange6((int)v, (int)v, proto, dir), b);
06422         return b;
06423         }
06424 #endif /* INET6 */
06425 
06426     case Q_GATEWAY:
06427         bpf_error("'gateway' requires a name");
06428         /* NOTREACHED */
06429 
06430     case Q_PROTO:
06431         return gen_proto((int)v, proto, dir);
06432 
06433     case Q_PROTOCHAIN:
06434         return gen_protochain((int)v, proto, dir);
06435 
06436     case Q_UNDEF:
06437         syntax();
06438         /* NOTREACHED */
06439 
06440     default:
06441         abort();
06442         /* NOTREACHED */
06443     }
06444     /* NOTREACHED */
06445 }
06446 
06447 #ifdef INET6
06448 struct block *
06449 gen_mcode6(s1, s2, masklen, q)
06450     register const char *s1, *s2;
06451     register int masklen;
06452     struct qual q;
06453 {
06454     struct addrinfo *res;
06455     struct in6_addr *addr;
06456     struct in6_addr mask;
06457     struct block *b;
06458     u_int32_t *a, *m;
06459 
06460     if (s2)
06461         bpf_error("no mask %s supported", s2);
06462 
06463     res = pcap_nametoaddrinfo(s1);
06464     if (!res)
06465         bpf_error("invalid ip6 address %s", s1);
06466     ai = res;
06467     if (res->ai_next)
06468         bpf_error("%s resolved to multiple address", s1);
06469     addr = &((struct sockaddr_in6 *)res->ai_addr)->sin6_addr;
06470 
06471     if (sizeof(mask) * 8 < masklen)
06472         bpf_error("mask length must be <= %u", (unsigned int)(sizeof(mask) * 8));
06473     memset(&mask, 0, sizeof(mask));
06474     memset(&mask, 0xff, masklen / 8);
06475     if (masklen % 8) {
06476         mask.s6_addr[masklen / 8] =
06477             (0xff << (8 - masklen % 8)) & 0xff;
06478     }
06479 
06480     a = (u_int32_t *)addr;
06481     m = (u_int32_t *)&mask;
06482     if ((a[0] & ~m[0]) || (a[1] & ~m[1])
06483      || (a[2] & ~m[2]) || (a[3] & ~m[3])) {
06484         bpf_error("non-network bits set in \"%s/%d\"", s1, masklen);
06485     }
06486 
06487     switch (q.addr) {
06488 
06489     case Q_DEFAULT:
06490     case Q_HOST:
06491         if (masklen != 128)
06492             bpf_error("Mask syntax for networks only");
06493         /* FALLTHROUGH */
06494 
06495     case Q_NET:
06496         b = gen_host6(addr, &mask, q.proto, q.dir, q.addr);
06497         ai = NULL;
06498         freeaddrinfo(res);
06499         return b;
06500 
06501     default:
06502         bpf_error("invalid qualifier against IPv6 address");
06503         /* NOTREACHED */
06504     }
06505     return NULL;
06506 }
06507 #endif /*INET6*/
06508 
06509 struct block *
06510 gen_ecode(eaddr, q)
06511     register const u_char *eaddr;
06512     struct qual q;
06513 {
06514     struct block *b, *tmp;
06515 
06516     if ((q.addr == Q_HOST || q.addr == Q_DEFAULT) && q.proto == Q_LINK) {
06517         switch (linktype) {
06518         case DLT_EN10MB:
06519             return gen_ehostop(eaddr, (int)q.dir);
06520         case DLT_FDDI:
06521             return gen_fhostop(eaddr, (int)q.dir);
06522         case DLT_IEEE802:
06523             return gen_thostop(eaddr, (int)q.dir);
06524         case DLT_IEEE802_11:
06525         case DLT_PRISM_HEADER:
06526         case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO_AVS:
06527         case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO:
06528         case DLT_PPI:
06529             return gen_wlanhostop(eaddr, (int)q.dir);
06530         case DLT_SUNATM:
06531             if (is_lane) {
06532                 /*
06533                  * Check that the packet doesn't begin with an
06534                  * LE Control marker.  (We've already generated
06535                  * a test for LANE.)
06536                  */
06537                 tmp = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, SUNATM_PKT_BEGIN_POS, BPF_H,
06538                     0xFF00);
06539                 gen_not(tmp);
06540 
06541                 /*
06542                  * Now check the MAC address.
06543                  */
06544                 b = gen_ehostop(eaddr, (int)q.dir);
06545                 gen_and(tmp, b);
06546                 return b;
06547             }
06548             break;
06549         case DLT_IP_OVER_FC:
06550             return gen_ipfchostop(eaddr, (int)q.dir);
06551         default:
06552             bpf_error("ethernet addresses supported only on ethernet/FDDI/token ring/802.11/ATM LANE/Fibre Channel");
06553             break;
06554         }
06555     }
06556     bpf_error("ethernet address used in non-ether expression");
06557     /* NOTREACHED */
06558     return NULL;
06559 }
06560 
06561 void
06562 sappend(s0, s1)
06563     struct slist *s0, *s1;
06564 {
06565     /*
06566      * This is definitely not the best way to do this, but the
06567      * lists will rarely get long.
06568      */
06569     while (s0->next)
06570         s0 = s0->next;
06571     s0->next = s1;
06572 }
06573 
06574 static struct slist *
06575 xfer_to_x(a)
06576     struct arth *a;
06577 {
06578     struct slist *s;
06579 
06580     s = new_stmt(BPF_LDX|BPF_MEM);
06581     s->s.k = a->regno;
06582     return s;
06583 }
06584 
06585 static struct slist *
06586 xfer_to_a(a)
06587     struct arth *a;
06588 {
06589     struct slist *s;
06590 
06591     s = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_MEM);
06592     s->s.k = a->regno;
06593     return s;
06594 }
06595 
06596 /*
06597  * Modify "index" to use the value stored into its register as an
06598  * offset relative to the beginning of the header for the protocol
06599  * "proto", and allocate a register and put an item "size" bytes long
06600  * (1, 2, or 4) at that offset into that register, making it the register
06601  * for "index".
06602  */
06603 struct arth *
06604 gen_load(proto, inst, size)
06605     int proto;
06606     struct arth *inst;
06607     int size;
06608 {
06609     struct slist *s, *tmp;
06610     struct block *b;
06611     int regno = alloc_reg();
06612 
06613     free_reg(inst->regno);
06614     switch (size) {
06615 
06616     default:
06617         bpf_error("data size must be 1, 2, or 4");
06618 
06619     case 1:
06620         size = BPF_B;
06621         break;
06622 
06623     case 2:
06624         size = BPF_H;
06625         break;
06626 
06627     case 4:
06628         size = BPF_W;
06629         break;
06630     }
06631     switch (proto) {
06632     default:
06633         bpf_error("unsupported index operation");
06634 
06635     case Q_RADIO:
06636         /*
06637          * The offset is relative to the beginning of the packet
06638          * data, if we have a radio header.  (If we don't, this
06639          * is an error.)
06640          */
06641         if (linktype != DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO_AVS &&
06642             linktype != DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO &&
06643             linktype != DLT_PRISM_HEADER)
06644             bpf_error("radio information not present in capture");
06645 
06646         /*
06647          * Load into the X register the offset computed into the
06648          * register specifed by "index".
06649          */
06650         s = xfer_to_x(inst);
06651 
06652         /*
06653          * Load the item at that offset.
06654          */
06655         tmp = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_IND|size);
06656         sappend(s, tmp);
06657         sappend(inst->s, s);
06658         break;
06659 
06660     case Q_LINK:
06661         /*
06662          * The offset is relative to the beginning of
06663          * the link-layer header.
06664          *
06665          * XXX - what about ATM LANE?  Should the index be
06666          * relative to the beginning of the AAL5 frame, so
06667          * that 0 refers to the beginning of the LE Control
06668          * field, or relative to the beginning of the LAN
06669          * frame, so that 0 refers, for Ethernet LANE, to
06670          * the beginning of the destination address?
06671          */
06672         s = gen_llprefixlen();
06673 
06674         /*
06675          * If "s" is non-null, it has code to arrange that the
06676          * X register contains the length of the prefix preceding
06677          * the link-layer header.  Add to it the offset computed
06678          * into the register specified by "index", and move that
06679          * into the X register.  Otherwise, just load into the X
06680          * register the offset computed into the register specifed
06681          * by "index".
06682          */
06683         if (s != NULL) {
06684             sappend(s, xfer_to_a(inst));
06685             sappend(s, new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_ADD|BPF_X));
06686             sappend(s, new_stmt(BPF_MISC|BPF_TAX));
06687         } else
06688             s = xfer_to_x(inst);
06689 
06690         /*
06691          * Load the item at the sum of the offset we've put in the
06692          * X register and the offset of the start of the link
06693          * layer header (which is 0 if the radio header is
06694          * variable-length; that header length is what we put
06695          * into the X register and then added to the index).
06696          */
06697         tmp = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_IND|size);
06698         tmp->s.k = off_ll;
06699         sappend(s, tmp);
06700         sappend(inst->s, s);
06701         break;
06702 
06703     case Q_IP:
06704     case Q_ARP:
06705     case Q_RARP:
06706     case Q_ATALK:
06707     case Q_DECNET:
06708     case Q_SCA:
06709     case Q_LAT:
06710     case Q_MOPRC:
06711     case Q_MOPDL:
06712 #ifdef INET6
06713     case Q_IPV6:
06714 #endif
06715         /*
06716          * The offset is relative to the beginning of
06717          * the network-layer header.
06718          * XXX - are there any cases where we want
06719          * off_nl_nosnap?
06720          */
06721         s = gen_off_macpl();
06722 
06723         /*
06724          * If "s" is non-null, it has code to arrange that the
06725          * X register contains the offset of the MAC-layer
06726          * payload.  Add to it the offset computed into the
06727          * register specified by "index", and move that into
06728          * the X register.  Otherwise, just load into the X
06729          * register the offset computed into the register specifed
06730          * by "index".
06731          */
06732         if (s != NULL) {
06733             sappend(s, xfer_to_a(inst));
06734             sappend(s, new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_ADD|BPF_X));
06735             sappend(s, new_stmt(BPF_MISC|BPF_TAX));
06736         } else
06737             s = xfer_to_x(inst);
06738 
06739         /*
06740          * Load the item at the sum of the offset we've put in the
06741          * X register, the offset of the start of the network
06742          * layer header from the beginning of the MAC-layer
06743          * payload, and the purported offset of the start of the
06744          * MAC-layer payload (which might be 0 if there's a
06745          * variable-length prefix before the link-layer header
06746          * or the link-layer header itself is variable-length;
06747          * the variable-length offset of the start of the
06748          * MAC-layer payload is what we put into the X register
06749          * and then added to the index).
06750          */
06751         tmp = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_IND|size);
06752         tmp->s.k = off_macpl + off_nl;
06753         sappend(s, tmp);
06754         sappend(inst->s, s);
06755 
06756         /*
06757          * Do the computation only if the packet contains
06758          * the protocol in question.
06759          */
06760         b = gen_proto_abbrev(proto);
06761         if (inst->b)
06762             gen_and(inst->b, b);
06763         inst->b = b;
06764         break;
06765 
06766     case Q_SCTP:
06767     case Q_TCP:
06768     case Q_UDP:
06769     case Q_ICMP:
06770     case Q_IGMP:
06771     case Q_IGRP:
06772     case Q_PIM:
06773     case Q_VRRP:
06774         /*
06775          * The offset is relative to the beginning of
06776          * the transport-layer header.
06777          *
06778          * Load the X register with the length of the IPv4 header
06779          * (plus the offset of the link-layer header, if it's
06780          * a variable-length header), in bytes.
06781          *
06782          * XXX - are there any cases where we want
06783          * off_nl_nosnap?
06784          * XXX - we should, if we're built with
06785          * IPv6 support, generate code to load either
06786          * IPv4, IPv6, or both, as appropriate.
06787          */
06788         s = gen_loadx_iphdrlen();
06789 
06790         /*
06791          * The X register now contains the sum of the length
06792          * of any variable-length header preceding the link-layer
06793          * header, any variable-length link-layer header, and the
06794          * length of the network-layer header.
06795          *
06796          * Load into the A register the offset relative to
06797          * the beginning of the transport layer header,
06798          * add the X register to that, move that to the
06799          * X register, and load with an offset from the
06800          * X register equal to the offset of the network
06801          * layer header relative to the beginning of
06802          * the MAC-layer payload plus the fixed-length
06803          * portion of the offset of the MAC-layer payload
06804          * from the beginning of the raw packet data.
06805          */
06806         sappend(s, xfer_to_a(inst));
06807         sappend(s, new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_ADD|BPF_X));
06808         sappend(s, new_stmt(BPF_MISC|BPF_TAX));
06809         sappend(s, tmp = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_IND|size));
06810         tmp->s.k = off_macpl + off_nl;
06811         sappend(inst->s, s);
06812 
06813         /*
06814          * Do the computation only if the packet contains
06815          * the protocol in question - which is true only
06816          * if this is an IP datagram and is the first or
06817          * only fragment of that datagram.
06818          */
06819         gen_and(gen_proto_abbrev(proto), b = gen_ipfrag());
06820         if (inst->b)
06821             gen_and(inst->b, b);
06822 #ifdef INET6
06823         gen_and(gen_proto_abbrev(Q_IP), b);
06824 #endif
06825         inst->b = b;
06826         break;
06827 #ifdef INET6
06828     case Q_ICMPV6:
06829         bpf_error("IPv6 upper-layer protocol is not supported by proto[x]");
06830         /*NOTREACHED*/
06831 #endif
06832     }
06833     inst->regno = regno;
06834     s = new_stmt(BPF_ST);
06835     s->s.k = regno;
06836     sappend(inst->s, s);
06837 
06838     return inst;
06839 }
06840 
06841 struct block *
06842 gen_relation(code, a0, a1, reversed)
06843     int code;
06844     struct arth *a0, *a1;
06845     int reversed;
06846 {
06847     struct slist *s0, *s1, *s2;
06848     struct block *b, *tmp;
06849 
06850     s0 = xfer_to_x(a1);
06851     s1 = xfer_to_a(a0);
06852     if (code == BPF_JEQ) {
06853         s2 = new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_SUB|BPF_X);
06854         b = new_block(JMP(code));
06855         sappend(s1, s2);
06856     }
06857     else
06858         b = new_block(BPF_JMP|code|BPF_X);
06859     if (reversed)
06860         gen_not(b);
06861 
06862     sappend(s0, s1);
06863     sappend(a1->s, s0);
06864     sappend(a0->s, a1->s);
06865 
06866     b->stmts = a0->s;
06867 
06868     free_reg(a0->regno);
06869     free_reg(a1->regno);
06870 
06871     /* 'and' together protocol checks */
06872     if (a0->b) {
06873         if (a1->b) {
06874             gen_and(a0->b, tmp = a1->b);
06875         }
06876         else
06877             tmp = a0->b;
06878     } else
06879         tmp = a1->b;
06880 
06881     if (tmp)
06882         gen_and(tmp, b);
06883 
06884     return b;
06885 }
06886 
06887 struct arth *
06888 gen_loadlen()
06889 {
06890     int regno = alloc_reg();
06891     struct arth *a = (struct arth *)newchunk(sizeof(*a));
06892     struct slist *s;
06893 
06894     s = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_LEN);
06895     s->next = new_stmt(BPF_ST);
06896     s->next->s.k = regno;
06897     a->s = s;
06898     a->regno = regno;
06899 
06900     return a;
06901 }
06902 
06903 struct arth *
06904 gen_loadi(val)
06905     int val;
06906 {
06907     struct arth *a;
06908     struct slist *s;
06909     int reg;
06910 
06911     a = (struct arth *)newchunk(sizeof(*a));
06912 
06913     reg = alloc_reg();
06914 
06915     s = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_IMM);
06916     s->s.k = val;
06917     s->next = new_stmt(BPF_ST);
06918     s->next->s.k = reg;
06919     a->s = s;
06920     a->regno = reg;
06921 
06922     return a;
06923 }
06924 
06925 struct arth *
06926 gen_neg(a)
06927     struct arth *a;
06928 {
06929     struct slist *s;
06930 
06931     s = xfer_to_a(a);
06932     sappend(a->s, s);
06933     s = new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_NEG);
06934     s->s.k = 0;
06935     sappend(a->s, s);
06936     s = new_stmt(BPF_ST);
06937     s->s.k = a->regno;
06938     sappend(a->s, s);
06939 
06940     return a;
06941 }
06942 
06943 struct arth *
06944 gen_arth(code, a0, a1)
06945     int code;
06946     struct arth *a0, *a1;
06947 {
06948     struct slist *s0, *s1, *s2;
06949 
06950     s0 = xfer_to_x(a1);
06951     s1 = xfer_to_a(a0);
06952     s2 = new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_X|code);
06953 
06954     sappend(s1, s2);
06955     sappend(s0, s1);
06956     sappend(a1->s, s0);
06957     sappend(a0->s, a1->s);
06958 
06959     free_reg(a0->regno);
06960     free_reg(a1->regno);
06961 
06962     s0 = new_stmt(BPF_ST);
06963     a0->regno = s0->s.k = alloc_reg();
06964     sappend(a0->s, s0);
06965 
06966     return a0;
06967 }
06968 
06969 /*
06970  * Here we handle simple allocation of the scratch registers.
06971  * If too many registers are alloc'd, the allocator punts.
06972  */
06973 static int regused[BPF_MEMWORDS];
06974 static int curreg;
06975 
06976 /*
06977  * Initialize the table of used registers and the current register.
06978  */
06979 static void
06980 init_regs()
06981 {
06982     curreg = 0;
06983     memset(regused, 0, sizeof regused);
06984 }
06985 
06986 /*
06987  * Return the next free register.
06988  */
06989 static int
06990 alloc_reg()
06991 {
06992     int n = BPF_MEMWORDS;
06993 
06994     while (--n >= 0) {
06995         if (regused[curreg])
06996             curreg = (curreg + 1) % BPF_MEMWORDS;
06997         else {
06998             regused[curreg] = 1;
06999             return curreg;
07000         }
07001     }
07002     bpf_error("too many registers needed to evaluate expression");
07003     /* NOTREACHED */
07004     return 0;
07005 }
07006 
07007 /*
07008  * Return a register to the table so it can
07009  * be used later.
07010  */
07011 static void
07012 free_reg(n)
07013     int n;
07014 {
07015     regused[n] = 0;
07016 }
07017 
07018 static struct block *
07019 gen_len(jmp, n)
07020     int jmp, n;
07021 {
07022     struct slist *s;
07023     struct block *b;
07024 
07025     s = new_stmt(BPF_LD|BPF_LEN);
07026     b = new_block(JMP(jmp));
07027     b->stmts = s;
07028     b->s.k = n;
07029 
07030     return b;
07031 }
07032 
07033 struct block *
07034 gen_greater(n)
07035     int n;
07036 {
07037     return gen_len(BPF_JGE, n);
07038 }
07039 
07040 /*
07041  * Actually, this is less than or equal.
07042  */
07043 struct block *
07044 gen_less(n)
07045     int n;
07046 {
07047     struct block *b;
07048 
07049     b = gen_len(BPF_JGT, n);
07050     gen_not(b);
07051 
07052     return b;
07053 }
07054 
07055 /*
07056  * This is for "byte {idx} {op} {val}"; "idx" is treated as relative to
07057  * the beginning of the link-layer header.
07058  * XXX - that means you can't test values in the radiotap header, but
07059  * as that header is difficult if not impossible to parse generally
07060  * without a loop, that might not be a severe problem.  A new keyword
07061  * "radio" could be added for that, although what you'd really want
07062  * would be a way of testing particular radio header values, which
07063  * would generate code appropriate to the radio header in question.
07064  */
07065 struct block *
07066 gen_byteop(op, idx, val)
07067     int op, idx, val;
07068 {
07069     struct block *b;
07070     struct slist *s;
07071 
07072     switch (op) {
07073     default:
07074         abort();
07075 
07076     case '=':
07077         return gen_cmp(OR_LINK, (u_int)idx, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)val);
07078 
07079     case '<':
07080         b = gen_cmp_lt(OR_LINK, (u_int)idx, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)val);
07081         return b;
07082 
07083     case '>':
07084         b = gen_cmp_gt(OR_LINK, (u_int)idx, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)val);
07085         return b;
07086 
07087     case '|':
07088         s = new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_OR|BPF_K);
07089         break;
07090 
07091     case '&':
07092         s = new_stmt(BPF_ALU|BPF_AND|BPF_K);
07093         break;
07094     }
07095     s->s.k = val;
07096     b = new_block(JMP(BPF_JEQ));
07097     b->stmts = s;
07098     gen_not(b);
07099 
07100     return b;
07101 }
07102 
07103 static u_char abroadcast[] = { 0x0 };
07104 
07105 struct block *
07106 gen_broadcast(proto)
07107     int proto;
07108 {
07109     bpf_u_int32 hostmask;
07110     struct block *b0, *b1, *b2;
07111     static u_char ebroadcast[] = { 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff };
07112 
07113     switch (proto) {
07114 
07115     case Q_DEFAULT:
07116     case Q_LINK:
07117         switch (linktype) {
07118         case DLT_ARCNET:
07119         case DLT_ARCNET_LINUX:
07120             return gen_ahostop(abroadcast, Q_DST);
07121         case DLT_EN10MB:
07122             return gen_ehostop(ebroadcast, Q_DST);
07123         case DLT_FDDI:
07124             return gen_fhostop(ebroadcast, Q_DST);
07125         case DLT_IEEE802:
07126             return gen_thostop(ebroadcast, Q_DST);
07127         case DLT_IEEE802_11:
07128         case DLT_PRISM_HEADER:
07129         case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO_AVS:
07130         case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO:
07131         case DLT_PPI:
07132             return gen_wlanhostop(ebroadcast, Q_DST);
07133         case DLT_IP_OVER_FC:
07134             return gen_ipfchostop(ebroadcast, Q_DST);
07135         case DLT_SUNATM:
07136             if (is_lane) {
07137                 /*
07138                  * Check that the packet doesn't begin with an
07139                  * LE Control marker.  (We've already generated
07140                  * a test for LANE.)
07141                  */
07142                 b1 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, SUNATM_PKT_BEGIN_POS,
07143                     BPF_H, 0xFF00);
07144                 gen_not(b1);
07145 
07146                 /*
07147                  * Now check the MAC address.
07148                  */
07149                 b0 = gen_ehostop(ebroadcast, Q_DST);
07150                 gen_and(b1, b0);
07151                 return b0;
07152             }
07153             break;
07154         default:
07155             bpf_error("not a broadcast link");
07156         }
07157         break;
07158 
07159     case Q_IP:
07160         /*
07161          * We treat a netmask of PCAP_NETMASK_UNKNOWN (0xffffffff)
07162          * as an indication that we don't know the netmask, and fail
07163          * in that case.
07164          */
07165         if (netmask == PCAP_NETMASK_UNKNOWN)
07166             bpf_error("netmask not known, so 'ip broadcast' not supported");
07167         b0 = gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_IP);
07168         hostmask = ~netmask;
07169         b1 = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, 16, BPF_W, (bpf_int32)0, hostmask);
07170         b2 = gen_mcmp(OR_NET, 16, BPF_W,
07171                   (bpf_int32)(~0 & hostmask), hostmask);
07172         gen_or(b1, b2);
07173         gen_and(b0, b2);
07174         return b2;
07175     }
07176     bpf_error("only link-layer/IP broadcast filters supported");
07177     /* NOTREACHED */
07178     return NULL;
07179 }
07180 
07181 /*
07182  * Generate code to test the low-order bit of a MAC address (that's
07183  * the bottom bit of the *first* byte).
07184  */
07185 static struct block *
07186 gen_mac_multicast(offset)
07187     int offset;
07188 {
07189     register struct block *b0;
07190     register struct slist *s;
07191 
07192     /* link[offset] & 1 != 0 */
07193     s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, offset, BPF_B);
07194     b0 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
07195     b0->s.k = 1;
07196     b0->stmts = s;
07197     return b0;
07198 }
07199 
07200 struct block *
07201 gen_multicast(proto)
07202     int proto;
07203 {
07204     register struct block *b0, *b1, *b2;
07205     register struct slist *s;
07206 
07207     switch (proto) {
07208 
07209     case Q_DEFAULT:
07210     case Q_LINK:
07211         switch (linktype) {
07212         case DLT_ARCNET:
07213         case DLT_ARCNET_LINUX:
07214             /* all ARCnet multicasts use the same address */
07215             return gen_ahostop(abroadcast, Q_DST);
07216         case DLT_EN10MB:
07217             /* ether[0] & 1 != 0 */
07218             return gen_mac_multicast(0);
07219         case DLT_FDDI:
07220             /*
07221              * XXX TEST THIS: MIGHT NOT PORT PROPERLY XXX
07222              *
07223              * XXX - was that referring to bit-order issues?
07224              */
07225             /* fddi[1] & 1 != 0 */
07226             return gen_mac_multicast(1);
07227         case DLT_IEEE802:
07228             /* tr[2] & 1 != 0 */
07229             return gen_mac_multicast(2);
07230         case DLT_IEEE802_11:
07231         case DLT_PRISM_HEADER:
07232         case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO_AVS:
07233         case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO:
07234         case DLT_PPI:
07235             /*
07236              * Oh, yuk.
07237              *
07238              *  For control frames, there is no DA.
07239              *
07240              *  For management frames, DA is at an
07241              *  offset of 4 from the beginning of
07242              *  the packet.
07243              *
07244              *  For data frames, DA is at an offset
07245              *  of 4 from the beginning of the packet
07246              *  if To DS is clear and at an offset of
07247              *  16 from the beginning of the packet
07248              *  if To DS is set.
07249              */
07250 
07251             /*
07252              * Generate the tests to be done for data frames.
07253              *
07254              * First, check for To DS set, i.e. "link[1] & 0x01".
07255              */
07256             s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 1, BPF_B);
07257             b1 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
07258             b1->s.k = 0x01; /* To DS */
07259             b1->stmts = s;
07260 
07261             /*
07262              * If To DS is set, the DA is at 16.
07263              */
07264             b0 = gen_mac_multicast(16);
07265             gen_and(b1, b0);
07266 
07267             /*
07268              * Now, check for To DS not set, i.e. check
07269              * "!(link[1] & 0x01)".
07270              */
07271             s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 1, BPF_B);
07272             b2 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
07273             b2->s.k = 0x01; /* To DS */
07274             b2->stmts = s;
07275             gen_not(b2);
07276 
07277             /*
07278              * If To DS is not set, the DA is at 4.
07279              */
07280             b1 = gen_mac_multicast(4);
07281             gen_and(b2, b1);
07282 
07283             /*
07284              * Now OR together the last two checks.  That gives
07285              * the complete set of checks for data frames.
07286              */
07287             gen_or(b1, b0);
07288 
07289             /*
07290              * Now check for a data frame.
07291              * I.e, check "link[0] & 0x08".
07292              */
07293             s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B);
07294             b1 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
07295             b1->s.k = 0x08;
07296             b1->stmts = s;
07297 
07298             /*
07299              * AND that with the checks done for data frames.
07300              */
07301             gen_and(b1, b0);
07302 
07303             /*
07304              * If the high-order bit of the type value is 0, this
07305              * is a management frame.
07306              * I.e, check "!(link[0] & 0x08)".
07307              */
07308             s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B);
07309             b2 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
07310             b2->s.k = 0x08;
07311             b2->stmts = s;
07312             gen_not(b2);
07313 
07314             /*
07315              * For management frames, the DA is at 4.
07316              */
07317             b1 = gen_mac_multicast(4);
07318             gen_and(b2, b1);
07319 
07320             /*
07321              * OR that with the checks done for data frames.
07322              * That gives the checks done for management and
07323              * data frames.
07324              */
07325             gen_or(b1, b0);
07326 
07327             /*
07328              * If the low-order bit of the type value is 1,
07329              * this is either a control frame or a frame
07330              * with a reserved type, and thus not a
07331              * frame with an SA.
07332              *
07333              * I.e., check "!(link[0] & 0x04)".
07334              */
07335             s = gen_load_a(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B);
07336             b1 = new_block(JMP(BPF_JSET));
07337             b1->s.k = 0x04;
07338             b1->stmts = s;
07339             gen_not(b1);
07340 
07341             /*
07342              * AND that with the checks for data and management
07343              * frames.
07344              */
07345             gen_and(b1, b0);
07346             return b0;
07347         case DLT_IP_OVER_FC:
07348             b0 = gen_mac_multicast(2);
07349             return b0;
07350         case DLT_SUNATM:
07351             if (is_lane) {
07352                 /*
07353                  * Check that the packet doesn't begin with an
07354                  * LE Control marker.  (We've already generated
07355                  * a test for LANE.)
07356                  */
07357                 b1 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, SUNATM_PKT_BEGIN_POS,
07358                     BPF_H, 0xFF00);
07359                 gen_not(b1);
07360 
07361                 /* ether[off_mac] & 1 != 0 */
07362                 b0 = gen_mac_multicast(off_mac);
07363                 gen_and(b1, b0);
07364                 return b0;
07365             }
07366             break;
07367         default:
07368             break;
07369         }
07370         /* Link not known to support multicasts */
07371         break;
07372 
07373     case Q_IP:
07374         b0 = gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_IP);
07375         b1 = gen_cmp_ge(OR_NET, 16, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)224);
07376         gen_and(b0, b1);
07377         return b1;
07378 
07379 #ifdef INET6
07380     case Q_IPV6:
07381         b0 = gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_IPV6);
07382         b1 = gen_cmp(OR_NET, 24, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)255);
07383         gen_and(b0, b1);
07384         return b1;
07385 #endif /* INET6 */
07386     }
07387     bpf_error("link-layer multicast filters supported only on ethernet/FDDI/token ring/ARCNET/802.11/ATM LANE/Fibre Channel");
07388     /* NOTREACHED */
07389     return NULL;
07390 }
07391 
07392 /*
07393  * generate command for inbound/outbound.  It's here so we can
07394  * make it link-type specific.  'dir' = 0 implies "inbound",
07395  * = 1 implies "outbound".
07396  */
07397 struct block *
07398 gen_inbound(dir)
07399     int dir;
07400 {
07401     register struct block *b0;
07402 
07403     /*
07404      * Only some data link types support inbound/outbound qualifiers.
07405      */
07406     switch (linktype) {
07407     case DLT_SLIP:
07408         b0 = gen_relation(BPF_JEQ,
07409               gen_load(Q_LINK, gen_loadi(0), 1),
07410               gen_loadi(0),
07411               dir);
07412         break;
07413 
07414     case DLT_IPNET:
07415         if (dir) {
07416             /* match outgoing packets */
07417             b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, 2, BPF_H, IPNET_OUTBOUND);
07418         } else {
07419             /* match incoming packets */
07420             b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, 2, BPF_H, IPNET_INBOUND);
07421         }
07422         break;
07423 
07424     case DLT_LINUX_SLL:
07425         if (dir) {
07426             /*
07427              * Match packets sent by this machine.
07428              */
07429             b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_H, LINUX_SLL_OUTGOING);
07430         } else {
07431             /*
07432              * Match packets sent to this machine.
07433              * (No broadcast or multicast packets, or
07434              * packets sent to some other machine and
07435              * received promiscuously.)
07436              *
07437              * XXX - packets sent to other machines probably
07438              * shouldn't be matched, but what about broadcast
07439              * or multicast packets we received?
07440              */
07441             b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_H, LINUX_SLL_HOST);
07442         }
07443         break;
07444 
07445 #ifdef HAVE_NET_PFVAR_H
07446     case DLT_PFLOG:
07447         b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, offsetof(struct pfloghdr, dir), BPF_B,
07448             (bpf_int32)((dir == 0) ? PF_IN : PF_OUT));
07449         break;
07450 #endif
07451 
07452     case DLT_PPP_PPPD:
07453         if (dir) {
07454             /* match outgoing packets */
07455             b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B, PPP_PPPD_OUT);
07456         } else {
07457             /* match incoming packets */
07458             b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B, PPP_PPPD_IN);
07459         }
07460         break;
07461 
07462         case DLT_JUNIPER_MFR:
07463         case DLT_JUNIPER_MLFR:
07464         case DLT_JUNIPER_MLPPP:
07465     case DLT_JUNIPER_ATM1:
07466     case DLT_JUNIPER_ATM2:
07467     case DLT_JUNIPER_PPPOE:
07468     case DLT_JUNIPER_PPPOE_ATM:
07469         case DLT_JUNIPER_GGSN:
07470         case DLT_JUNIPER_ES:
07471         case DLT_JUNIPER_MONITOR:
07472         case DLT_JUNIPER_SERVICES:
07473         case DLT_JUNIPER_ETHER:
07474         case DLT_JUNIPER_PPP:
07475         case DLT_JUNIPER_FRELAY:
07476         case DLT_JUNIPER_CHDLC:
07477         case DLT_JUNIPER_VP:
07478         case DLT_JUNIPER_ST:
07479         case DLT_JUNIPER_ISM:
07480         /* juniper flags (including direction) are stored
07481          * the byte after the 3-byte magic number */
07482         if (dir) {
07483             /* match outgoing packets */
07484             b0 = gen_mcmp(OR_LINK, 3, BPF_B, 0, 0x01);
07485         } else {
07486             /* match incoming packets */
07487             b0 = gen_mcmp(OR_LINK, 3, BPF_B, 1, 0x01);
07488         }
07489         break;
07490 
07491     default:
07492         bpf_error("inbound/outbound not supported on linktype %d",
07493             linktype);
07494         b0 = NULL;
07495         /* NOTREACHED */
07496     }
07497     return (b0);
07498 }
07499 
07500 #ifdef HAVE_NET_PFVAR_H
07501 /* PF firewall log matched interface */
07502 struct block *
07503 gen_pf_ifname(const char *ifname)
07504 {
07505     struct block *b0;
07506     u_int len, off;
07507 
07508     if (linktype != DLT_PFLOG) {
07509         bpf_error("ifname supported only on PF linktype");
07510         /* NOTREACHED */
07511     }
07512     len = sizeof(((struct pfloghdr *)0)->ifname);
07513     off = offsetof(struct pfloghdr, ifname);
07514     if (strlen(ifname) >= len) {
07515         bpf_error("ifname interface names can only be %d characters",
07516             len-1);
07517         /* NOTREACHED */
07518     }
07519     b0 = gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, off, strlen(ifname), (const u_char *)ifname);
07520     return (b0);
07521 }
07522 
07523 /* PF firewall log ruleset name */
07524 struct block *
07525 gen_pf_ruleset(char *ruleset)
07526 {
07527     struct block *b0;
07528 
07529     if (linktype != DLT_PFLOG) {
07530         bpf_error("ruleset supported only on PF linktype");
07531         /* NOTREACHED */
07532     }
07533 
07534     if (strlen(ruleset) >= sizeof(((struct pfloghdr *)0)->ruleset)) {
07535         bpf_error("ruleset names can only be %ld characters",
07536             (long)(sizeof(((struct pfloghdr *)0)->ruleset) - 1));
07537         /* NOTREACHED */
07538     }
07539 
07540     b0 = gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, offsetof(struct pfloghdr, ruleset),
07541         strlen(ruleset), (const u_char *)ruleset);
07542     return (b0);
07543 }

07555
