07658 /* IEEE 802.11 wireless header */
07659 struct block *
07660 gen_p80211_type(int type, int mask)
07661 {
07662     struct block *b0;
07663 
07664     switch (linktype) {
07665 
07666     case DLT_IEEE802_11:
07667     case DLT_PRISM_HEADER:
07668     case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO_AVS:
07669     case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO:
07670         b0 = gen_mcmp(OR_LINK, 0, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)type,
07671             (bpf_int32)mask);
07672         break;
07673 
07674     default:
07675         bpf_error("802.11 link-layer types supported only on 802.11");
07676         /* NOTREACHED */
07677     }
07678 
07679     return (b0);
07680 }
07681 
07682 struct block *
07683 gen_p80211_fcdir(int fcdir)
07684 {
07685     struct block *b0;
07686 
07687     switch (linktype) {
07688 
07689     case DLT_IEEE802_11:
07690     case DLT_PRISM_HEADER:
07691     case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO_AVS:
07692     case DLT_IEEE802_11_RADIO:
07693         break;
07694 
07695     default:
07696         bpf_error("frame direction supported only with 802.11 headers");
07697         /* NOTREACHED */
07698     }
07699 
07700     b0 = gen_mcmp(OR_LINK, 1, BPF_B, (bpf_int32)fcdir,
07701         (bpf_u_int32)IEEE80211_FC1_DIR_MASK);
07702 
07703     return (b0);
07704 }
07705 
07706 struct block *
07707 gen_acode(eaddr, q)
07708     register const u_char *eaddr;
07709     struct qual q;
07710 {
07711     switch (linktype) {
07712 
07713     case DLT_ARCNET:
07714     case DLT_ARCNET_LINUX:
07715         if ((q.addr == Q_HOST || q.addr == Q_DEFAULT) &&
07716             q.proto == Q_LINK)
07717             return (gen_ahostop(eaddr, (int)q.dir));
07718         else {
07719             bpf_error("ARCnet address used in non-arc expression");
07720             /* NOTREACHED */
07721         }
07722         break;
07723 
07724     default:
07725         bpf_error("aid supported only on ARCnet");
07726         /* NOTREACHED */
07727     }
07728     bpf_error("ARCnet address used in non-arc expression");
07729     /* NOTREACHED */
07730     return NULL;
07731 }
07732 
07733 static struct block *
07734 gen_ahostop(eaddr, dir)
07735     register const u_char *eaddr;
07736     register int dir;
07737 {
07738     register struct block *b0, *b1;
07739 
07740     switch (dir) {
07741     /* src comes first, different from Ethernet */
07742     case Q_SRC:
07743         return gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 0, 1, eaddr);
07744 
07745     case Q_DST:
07746         return gen_bcmp(OR_LINK, 1, 1, eaddr);
07747 
07748     case Q_AND:
07749         b0 = gen_ahostop(eaddr, Q_SRC);
07750         b1 = gen_ahostop(eaddr, Q_DST);
07751         gen_and(b0, b1);
07752         return b1;
07753 
07754     case Q_DEFAULT:
07755     case Q_OR:
07756         b0 = gen_ahostop(eaddr, Q_SRC);
07757         b1 = gen_ahostop(eaddr, Q_DST);
07758         gen_or(b0, b1);
07759         return b1;
07760     }
07761     abort();
07762     /* NOTREACHED */
07763 }
07764 
07765 /*
07766  * support IEEE 802.1Q VLAN trunk over ethernet
07767  */
07768 struct block *
07769 gen_vlan(vlan_num)
07770     int vlan_num;
07771 {
07772     struct  block   *b0, *b1;
07773 
07774     /* can't check for VLAN-encapsulated packets inside MPLS */
07775     if (label_stack_depth > 0)
07776         bpf_error("no VLAN match after MPLS");
07777 
07778     /*
07779      * Check for a VLAN packet, and then change the offsets to point
07780      * to the type and data fields within the VLAN packet.  Just
07781      * increment the offsets, so that we can support a hierarchy, e.g.
07782      * "vlan 300 && vlan 200" to capture VLAN 200 encapsulated within
07783      * VLAN 100.
07784      *
07785      * XXX - this is a bit of a kludge.  If we were to split the
07786      * compiler into a parser that parses an expression and
07787      * generates an expression tree, and a code generator that
07788      * takes an expression tree (which could come from our
07789      * parser or from some other parser) and generates BPF code,
07790      * we could perhaps make the offsets parameters of routines
07791      * and, in the handler for an "AND" node, pass to subnodes
07792      * other than the VLAN node the adjusted offsets.
07793      *
07794      * This would mean that "vlan" would, instead of changing the
07795      * behavior of *all* tests after it, change only the behavior
07796      * of tests ANDed with it.  That would change the documented
07797      * semantics of "vlan", which might break some expressions.
07798      * However, it would mean that "(vlan and ip) or ip" would check
07799      * both for VLAN-encapsulated IP and IP-over-Ethernet, rather than
07800      * checking only for VLAN-encapsulated IP, so that could still
07801      * be considered worth doing; it wouldn't break expressions
07802      * that are of the form "vlan and ..." or "vlan N and ...",
07803      * which I suspect are the most common expressions involving
07804      * "vlan".  "vlan or ..." doesn't necessarily do what the user
07805      * would really want, now, as all the "or ..." tests would
07806      * be done assuming a VLAN, even though the "or" could be viewed
07807      * as meaning "or, if this isn't a VLAN packet...".
07808      */
07809     orig_nl = off_nl;
07810 
07811     switch (linktype) {
07812 
07813     case DLT_EN10MB:
07814         /* check for VLAN */
07815         b0 = gen_cmp(OR_LINK, off_linktype, BPF_H,
07816             (bpf_int32)ETHERTYPE_8021Q);
07817 
07818         /* If a specific VLAN is requested, check VLAN id */
07819         if (vlan_num >= 0) {
07820             b1 = gen_mcmp(OR_MACPL, 0, BPF_H,
07821                 (bpf_int32)vlan_num, 0x0fff);
07822             gen_and(b0, b1);
07823             b0 = b1;
07824         }
07825 
07826         off_macpl += 4;
07827         off_linktype += 4;
07828 #if 0
07829         off_nl_nosnap += 4;
07830         off_nl += 4;
07831 #endif
07832         break;
07833 
07834     default:
07835         bpf_error("no VLAN support for data link type %d",
07836               linktype);
07837         /*NOTREACHED*/
07838     }
07839 
07840     return (b0);
07841 }
07842 
07843 /*
07844  * support for MPLS
07845  */
07846 struct block *
07847 gen_mpls(label_num)
07848     int label_num;
07849 {
07850     struct  block   *b0,*b1;
07851 
07852     /*
07853      * Change the offsets to point to the type and data fields within
07854      * the MPLS packet.  Just increment the offsets, so that we
07855      * can support a hierarchy, e.g. "mpls 100000 && mpls 1024" to
07856      * capture packets with an outer label of 100000 and an inner
07857      * label of 1024.
07858      *
07859      * XXX - this is a bit of a kludge.  See comments in gen_vlan().
07860      */
07861         orig_nl = off_nl;
07862 
07863         if (label_stack_depth > 0) {
07864             /* just match the bottom-of-stack bit clear */
07865             b0 = gen_mcmp(OR_MACPL, orig_nl-2, BPF_B, 0, 0x01);
07866         } else {
07867             /*
07868              * Indicate that we're checking MPLS-encapsulated headers,
07869              * to make sure higher level code generators don't try to
07870              * match against IP-related protocols such as Q_ARP, Q_RARP
07871              * etc.
07872              */
07873             switch (linktype) {
07874                 
07875             case DLT_C_HDLC: /* fall through */
07876             case DLT_EN10MB:
07877                     b0 = gen_linktype(ETHERTYPE_MPLS);
07878                     break;
07879                 
07880             case DLT_PPP:
07881                     b0 = gen_linktype(PPP_MPLS_UCAST);
07882                     break;
07883                 
07884                     /* FIXME add other DLT_s ...
07885                      * for Frame-Relay/and ATM this may get messy due to SNAP headers
07886                      * leave it for now */
07887                 
07888             default:
07889                     bpf_error("no MPLS support for data link type %d",
07890                           linktype);
07891                     b0 = NULL;
07892                     /*NOTREACHED*/
07893                     break;
07894             }
07895         }
07896 
07897     /* If a specific MPLS label is requested, check it */
07898     if (label_num >= 0) {
07899         label_num = label_num << 12; /* label is shifted 12 bits on the wire */
07900         b1 = gen_mcmp(OR_MACPL, orig_nl, BPF_W, (bpf_int32)label_num,
07901             0xfffff000); /* only compare the first 20 bits */
07902         gen_and(b0, b1);
07903         b0 = b1;
07904     }
07905 
07906         off_nl_nosnap += 4;
07907         off_nl += 4;
07908         label_stack_depth++;
07909     return (b0);
07910 }
07911 
07912 /*
07913  * Support PPPOE discovery and session.
07914  */
07915 struct block *
07916 gen_pppoed()
07917 {
07918     /* check for PPPoE discovery */
07919     return gen_linktype((bpf_int32)ETHERTYPE_PPPOED);
07920 }
07921 
07922 struct block *
07923 gen_pppoes()
07924 {
07925     struct block *b0;
07926 
07927     /*
07928      * Test against the PPPoE session link-layer type.
07929      */
07930     b0 = gen_linktype((bpf_int32)ETHERTYPE_PPPOES);
07931 
07932     /*
07933      * Change the offsets to point to the type and data fields within
07934      * the PPP packet, and note that this is PPPoE rather than
07935      * raw PPP.
07936      *
07937      * XXX - this is a bit of a kludge.  If we were to split the
07938      * compiler into a parser that parses an expression and
07939      * generates an expression tree, and a code generator that
07940      * takes an expression tree (which could come from our
07941      * parser or from some other parser) and generates BPF code,
07942      * we could perhaps make the offsets parameters of routines
07943      * and, in the handler for an "AND" node, pass to subnodes
07944      * other than the PPPoE node the adjusted offsets.
07945      *
07946      * This would mean that "pppoes" would, instead of changing the
07947      * behavior of *all* tests after it, change only the behavior
07948      * of tests ANDed with it.  That would change the documented
07949      * semantics of "pppoes", which might break some expressions.
07950      * However, it would mean that "(pppoes and ip) or ip" would check
07951      * both for VLAN-encapsulated IP and IP-over-Ethernet, rather than
07952      * checking only for VLAN-encapsulated IP, so that could still
07953      * be considered worth doing; it wouldn't break expressions
07954      * that are of the form "pppoes and ..." which I suspect are the
07955      * most common expressions involving "pppoes".  "pppoes or ..."
07956      * doesn't necessarily do what the user would really want, now,
07957      * as all the "or ..." tests would be done assuming PPPoE, even
07958      * though the "or" could be viewed as meaning "or, if this isn't
07959      * a PPPoE packet...".
07960      */
07961     orig_linktype = off_linktype;   /* save original values */
07962     orig_nl = off_nl;
07963     is_pppoes = 1;
07964 
07965     /*
07966      * The "network-layer" protocol is PPPoE, which has a 6-byte
07967      * PPPoE header, followed by a PPP packet.
07968      *
07969      * There is no HDLC encapsulation for the PPP packet (it's
07970      * encapsulated in PPPoES instead), so the link-layer type
07971      * starts at the first byte of the PPP packet.  For PPPoE,
07972      * that offset is relative to the beginning of the total
07973      * link-layer payload, including any 802.2 LLC header, so
07974      * it's 6 bytes past off_nl.
07975      */
07976     off_linktype = off_nl + 6;
07977 
07978     /*
07979      * The network-layer offsets are relative to the beginning
07980      * of the MAC-layer payload; that's past the 6-byte
07981      * PPPoE header and the 2-byte PPP header.
07982      */
07983     off_nl = 6+2;
07984     off_nl_nosnap = 6+2;
07985 
07986     return b0;
07987 }
07988 
07989 struct block *
07990 gen_atmfield_code(atmfield, jvalue, jtype, reverse)
07991     int atmfield;
07992     bpf_int32 jvalue;
07993     bpf_u_int32 jtype;
07994     int reverse;
07995 {
07996     struct block *b0;
07997 
07998     switch (atmfield) {
07999 
08000     case A_VPI:
08001         if (!is_atm)
08002             bpf_error("'vpi' supported only on raw ATM");
08003         if (off_vpi == (u_int)-1)
08004             abort();
08005         b0 = gen_ncmp(OR_LINK, off_vpi, BPF_B, 0xffffffff, jtype,
08006             reverse, jvalue);
08007         break;
08008 
08009     case A_VCI:
08010         if (!is_atm)
08011             bpf_error("'vci' supported only on raw ATM");
08012         if (off_vci == (u_int)-1)
08013             abort();
08014         b0 = gen_ncmp(OR_LINK, off_vci, BPF_H, 0xffffffff, jtype,
08015             reverse, jvalue);
08016         break;
08017 
08018     case A_PROTOTYPE:
08019         if (off_proto == (u_int)-1)
08020             abort();    /* XXX - this isn't on FreeBSD */
08021         b0 = gen_ncmp(OR_LINK, off_proto, BPF_B, 0x0f, jtype,
08022             reverse, jvalue);
08023         break;
08024 
08025     case A_MSGTYPE:
08026         if (off_payload == (u_int)-1)
08027             abort();
08028         b0 = gen_ncmp(OR_LINK, off_payload + MSG_TYPE_POS, BPF_B,
08029             0xffffffff, jtype, reverse, jvalue);
08030         break;
08031 
08032     case A_CALLREFTYPE:
08033         if (!is_atm)
08034             bpf_error("'callref' supported only on raw ATM");
08035         if (off_proto == (u_int)-1)
08036             abort();
08037         b0 = gen_ncmp(OR_LINK, off_proto, BPF_B, 0xffffffff,
08038             jtype, reverse, jvalue);
08039         break;
08040 
08041     default:
08042         abort();
08043     }
08044     return b0;
08045 }
08046 
08047 struct block *
08048 gen_atmtype_abbrev(type)
08049     int type;
08050 {
08051     struct block *b0, *b1;
08052 
08053     switch (type) {
08054 
08055     case A_METAC:
08056         /* Get all packets in Meta signalling Circuit */
08057         if (!is_atm)
08058             bpf_error("'metac' supported only on raw ATM");
08059         b0 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VPI, 0, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08060         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VCI, 1, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08061         gen_and(b0, b1);
08062         break;
08063 
08064     case A_BCC:
08065         /* Get all packets in Broadcast Circuit*/
08066         if (!is_atm)
08067             bpf_error("'bcc' supported only on raw ATM");
08068         b0 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VPI, 0, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08069         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VCI, 2, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08070         gen_and(b0, b1);
08071         break;
08072 
08073     case A_OAMF4SC:
08074         /* Get all cells in Segment OAM F4 circuit*/
08075         if (!is_atm)
08076             bpf_error("'oam4sc' supported only on raw ATM");
08077         b0 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VPI, 0, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08078         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VCI, 3, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08079         gen_and(b0, b1);
08080         break;
08081 
08082     case A_OAMF4EC:
08083         /* Get all cells in End-to-End OAM F4 Circuit*/
08084         if (!is_atm)
08085             bpf_error("'oam4ec' supported only on raw ATM");
08086         b0 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VPI, 0, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08087         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VCI, 4, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08088         gen_and(b0, b1);
08089         break;
08090 
08091     case A_SC:
08092         /*  Get all packets in connection Signalling Circuit */
08093         if (!is_atm)
08094             bpf_error("'sc' supported only on raw ATM");
08095         b0 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VPI, 0, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08096         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VCI, 5, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08097         gen_and(b0, b1);
08098         break;
08099 
08100     case A_ILMIC:
08101         /* Get all packets in ILMI Circuit */
08102         if (!is_atm)
08103             bpf_error("'ilmic' supported only on raw ATM");
08104         b0 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VPI, 0, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08105         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VCI, 16, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08106         gen_and(b0, b1);
08107         break;
08108 
08109     case A_LANE:
08110         /* Get all LANE packets */
08111         if (!is_atm)
08112             bpf_error("'lane' supported only on raw ATM");
08113         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_PROTOTYPE, PT_LANE, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08114 
08115         /*
08116          * Arrange that all subsequent tests assume LANE
08117          * rather than LLC-encapsulated packets, and set
08118          * the offsets appropriately for LANE-encapsulated
08119          * Ethernet.
08120          *
08121          * "off_mac" is the offset of the Ethernet header,
08122          * which is 2 bytes past the ATM pseudo-header
08123          * (skipping the pseudo-header and 2-byte LE Client
08124          * field).  The other offsets are Ethernet offsets
08125          * relative to "off_mac".
08126          */
08127         is_lane = 1;
08128         off_mac = off_payload + 2;  /* MAC header */
08129         off_linktype = off_mac + 12;
08130         off_macpl = off_mac + 14;   /* Ethernet */
08131         off_nl = 0;         /* Ethernet II */
08132         off_nl_nosnap = 3;      /* 802.3+802.2 */
08133         break;
08134 
08135     case A_LLC:
08136         /* Get all LLC-encapsulated packets */
08137         if (!is_atm)
08138             bpf_error("'llc' supported only on raw ATM");
08139         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_PROTOTYPE, PT_LLC, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08140         is_lane = 0;
08141         break;
08142 
08143     default:
08144         abort();
08145     }
08146     return b1;
08147 }
08148 
08149 /* 
08150  * Filtering for MTP2 messages based on li value
08151  * FISU, length is null
08152  * LSSU, length is 1 or 2
08153  * MSU, length is 3 or more
08154  */
08155 struct block *
08156 gen_mtp2type_abbrev(type)
08157     int type;
08158 {
08159     struct block *b0, *b1;
08160 
08161     switch (type) {
08162 
08163     case M_FISU:
08164         if ( (linktype != DLT_MTP2) &&
08165              (linktype != DLT_ERF) &&
08166              (linktype != DLT_MTP2_WITH_PHDR) )
08167             bpf_error("'fisu' supported only on MTP2");
08168         /* gen_ncmp(offrel, offset, size, mask, jtype, reverse, value) */
08169         b0 = gen_ncmp(OR_PACKET, off_li, BPF_B, 0x3f, BPF_JEQ, 0, 0);
08170         break;
08171 
08172     case M_LSSU:
08173         if ( (linktype != DLT_MTP2) &&
08174              (linktype != DLT_ERF) &&
08175              (linktype != DLT_MTP2_WITH_PHDR) )
08176             bpf_error("'lssu' supported only on MTP2");
08177         b0 = gen_ncmp(OR_PACKET, off_li, BPF_B, 0x3f, BPF_JGT, 1, 2);
08178         b1 = gen_ncmp(OR_PACKET, off_li, BPF_B, 0x3f, BPF_JGT, 0, 0);
08179         gen_and(b1, b0);
08180         break;
08181 
08182     case M_MSU:
08183         if ( (linktype != DLT_MTP2) &&
08184              (linktype != DLT_ERF) &&
08185              (linktype != DLT_MTP2_WITH_PHDR) )
08186             bpf_error("'msu' supported only on MTP2");
08187         b0 = gen_ncmp(OR_PACKET, off_li, BPF_B, 0x3f, BPF_JGT, 0, 2);
08188         break;
08189 
08190     default:
08191         abort();
08192     }
08193     return b0;
08194 }
08195 
08196 struct block *
08197 gen_mtp3field_code(mtp3field, jvalue, jtype, reverse)
08198     int mtp3field;
08199     bpf_u_int32 jvalue;
08200     bpf_u_int32 jtype;
08201     int reverse;
08202 {
08203     struct block *b0;
08204     bpf_u_int32 val1 , val2 , val3;
08205 
08206     switch (mtp3field) {
08207 
08208     case M_SIO:
08209         if (off_sio == (u_int)-1)
08210             bpf_error("'sio' supported only on SS7");
08211         /* sio coded on 1 byte so max value 255 */
08212         if(jvalue > 255)
08213                 bpf_error("sio value %u too big; max value = 255",
08214                     jvalue);
08215         b0 = gen_ncmp(OR_PACKET, off_sio, BPF_B, 0xffffffff,
08216             (u_int)jtype, reverse, (u_int)jvalue);
08217         break;
08218 
08219         case M_OPC:
08220             if (off_opc == (u_int)-1)
08221             bpf_error("'opc' supported only on SS7");
08222         /* opc coded on 14 bits so max value 16383 */
08223         if (jvalue > 16383)
08224                 bpf_error("opc value %u too big; max value = 16383",
08225                     jvalue);
08226         /* the following instructions are made to convert jvalue
08227          * to the form used to write opc in an ss7 message*/
08228         val1 = jvalue & 0x00003c00;
08229         val1 = val1 >>10;
08230         val2 = jvalue & 0x000003fc;
08231         val2 = val2 <<6;
08232         val3 = jvalue & 0x00000003;
08233         val3 = val3 <<22;
08234         jvalue = val1 + val2 + val3;
08235         b0 = gen_ncmp(OR_PACKET, off_opc, BPF_W, 0x00c0ff0f,
08236             (u_int)jtype, reverse, (u_int)jvalue);
08237         break;
08238 
08239     case M_DPC:
08240             if (off_dpc == (u_int)-1)
08241             bpf_error("'dpc' supported only on SS7");
08242         /* dpc coded on 14 bits so max value 16383 */
08243         if (jvalue > 16383)
08244                 bpf_error("dpc value %u too big; max value = 16383",
08245                     jvalue);
08246         /* the following instructions are made to convert jvalue
08247          * to the forme used to write dpc in an ss7 message*/
08248         val1 = jvalue & 0x000000ff;
08249         val1 = val1 << 24;
08250         val2 = jvalue & 0x00003f00;
08251         val2 = val2 << 8;
08252         jvalue = val1 + val2;
08253         b0 = gen_ncmp(OR_PACKET, off_dpc, BPF_W, 0xff3f0000,
08254             (u_int)jtype, reverse, (u_int)jvalue);
08255         break;
08256 
08257     case M_SLS:
08258             if (off_sls == (u_int)-1)
08259             bpf_error("'sls' supported only on SS7");
08260         /* sls coded on 4 bits so max value 15 */
08261         if (jvalue > 15)
08262                  bpf_error("sls value %u too big; max value = 15",
08263                      jvalue);
08264         /* the following instruction is made to convert jvalue
08265          * to the forme used to write sls in an ss7 message*/
08266         jvalue = jvalue << 4;
08267         b0 = gen_ncmp(OR_PACKET, off_sls, BPF_B, 0xf0,
08268             (u_int)jtype,reverse, (u_int)jvalue);
08269         break;
08270 
08271     default:
08272         abort();
08273     }
08274     return b0;
08275 }

08277 static struct block *
08278 gen_msg_abbrev(type)
08279     int type;
08280 {
08281     struct block *b1;
08282 
08283     /*
08284      * Q.2931 signalling protocol messages for handling virtual circuits
08285      * establishment and teardown
08286      */
08287     switch (type) {
08288 
08289     case A_SETUP:
08290         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_MSGTYPE, SETUP, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08291         break;
08292 
08293     case A_CALLPROCEED:
08294         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_MSGTYPE, CALL_PROCEED, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08295         break;
08296 
08297     case A_CONNECT:
08298         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_MSGTYPE, CONNECT, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08299         break;
08300 
08301     case A_CONNECTACK:
08302         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_MSGTYPE, CONNECT_ACK, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08303         break;
08304 
08305     case A_RELEASE:
08306         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_MSGTYPE, RELEASE, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08307         break;
08308 
08309     case A_RELEASE_DONE:
08310         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_MSGTYPE, RELEASE_DONE, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08311         break;
08312 
08313     default:
08314         abort();
08315     }
08316     return b1;
08317 }

08319 struct block *
08320 gen_atmmulti_abbrev(type)
08321     int type;
08322 {
08323     struct block *b0, *b1;
08324 
08325     switch (type) {
08326 
08327     case A_OAM:
08328         if (!is_atm)
08329             bpf_error("'oam' supported only on raw ATM");
08330         b1 = gen_atmmulti_abbrev(A_OAMF4);
08331         break;
08332 
08333     case A_OAMF4:
08334         if (!is_atm)
08335             bpf_error("'oamf4' supported only on raw ATM");
08336         /* OAM F4 type */
08337         b0 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VCI, 3, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08338         b1 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VCI, 4, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08339         gen_or(b0, b1);
08340         b0 = gen_atmfield_code(A_VPI, 0, BPF_JEQ, 0);
08341         gen_and(b0, b1);
08342         break;
08343 
08344     case A_CONNECTMSG:
08345         /*
08346          * Get Q.2931 signalling messages for switched
08347          * virtual connection
08348          */
08349         if (!is_atm)
08350             bpf_error("'connectmsg' supported only on raw ATM");
08351         b0 = gen_msg_abbrev(A_SETUP);
08352         b1 = gen_msg_abbrev(A_CALLPROCEED);
08353         gen_or(b0, b1);
08354         b0 = gen_msg_abbrev(A_CONNECT);
08355         gen_or(b0, b1);
08356         b0 = gen_msg_abbrev(A_CONNECTACK);
08357         gen_or(b0, b1);
08358         b0 = gen_msg_abbrev(A_RELEASE);
08359         gen_or(b0, b1);
08360         b0 = gen_msg_abbrev(A_RELEASE_DONE);
08361         gen_or(b0, b1);
08362         b0 = gen_atmtype_abbrev(A_SC);
08363         gen_and(b0, b1);
08364         break;
08365 
08366     case A_METACONNECT:
08367         if (!is_atm)
08368             bpf_error("'metaconnect' supported only on raw ATM");
08369         b0 = gen_msg_abbrev(A_SETUP);
08370         b1 = gen_msg_abbrev(A_CALLPROCEED);
08371         gen_or(b0, b1);
08372         b0 = gen_msg_abbrev(A_CONNECT);
08373         gen_or(b0, b1);
08374         b0 = gen_msg_abbrev(A_RELEASE);
08375         gen_or(b0, b1);
08376         b0 = gen_msg_abbrev(A_RELEASE_DONE);
08377         gen_or(b0, b1);
08378         b0 = gen_atmtype_abbrev(A_METAC);
08379         gen_and(b0, b1);
08380         break;
08381 
08382     default:
08383         abort();
08384     }
08385     return b1;
08386 }
